Our ESG Foundation:Strategy, Purpose & Progress
Himadri Speciality Chemical Limited remains committed 
to responsible growth by embedding sustainability 
into its business model. Our ESG strategy, "Together 
Towards Tomorrow," is designed to drive environmental 
stewardship, social well-being for people/communities, 
continuous value creation for stakeholders, and ethical 
governance. This strategy covers not only internal 
operations but also those of our value chain partners.
Himadri delivers sustainable, value-added solutions that 
address evolving customer needs. This commitment is 
embodied in the Company’s purpose: ‘Excelling while 
innovating’.  Himadri extends beyond carbon chemistry 
to build competencies, perspectives, and partnerships. 
By leveraging its resident expertise and collaborations, 
Himadri is empowered to lead, create economic value, 
protect the environment, and enrich society.
In line with its commitment, the company has embedded 
Environmental, Social, and Governance (ESG) principles 
into its operations. As a forward-thinking organization, 
Himadri is shaping the future through strategic sector 
choices, innovative products, efficient processes, and 
responsible practices.
At Himadri, our core philosophy revolves around 
sustainability and responsibility, ensuring both short-
term and long-term value creation. However, the essence 
of our progress is captured in a single, powerful word—
"together."

Internal collaboration – At Himadri, we believe that true

This integrated approach allows us to drive breakthrough 
solutions, optimize operational efficiency, and respond 
proactively to the evolving needs of our stakeholders. 
By

and

we continuously push the boundaries of product

Through this alignment of human potential and scientific 
innovation, Himadri delivers holistic and future-ready 
solutions that create lasting value for customers, partners, 
communities, and the environment.
External association – Himadri is driven by a bold and 
inspiring vision—to enhance lives beyond expectations 
and shape a future where humanity and nature coexist 
in harmony. This commitment is not just aspirational; it is 
embedded in every aspect of how we operate, innovate, 
and engage with the world around us.
We work tirelessly to create positive, lasting impacts by 
aligning our business strategies with the broader goals 
of social well-being and environmental stewardship. Our 
efforts extend far beyond product excellence—we actively 
seek to enrich quality of life, empower communities, and 
contribute to a more sustainable and inclusive world.
Through 
meaningful 
stakeholder 
engagement, 
we 
foster open dialogue and collaborative partnerships, 
encouraging a deeper understanding of shared challenges 
and opportunities. We believe that transparency and 
knowledge-sharing are essential to build trust and 
achieve collective progress. By sharing valuable insights, 
technological advancements, and sustainability practices, 
we strive to uplift the communities we serve and inspire 
broader societal change.
Himadri also collaborates with global partners, industry 
leaders, and knowledge experts, tapping into diverse 
expertise to drive innovation, accelerate sustainable

other industries by pioneering technologies, furthering

Sustainability is not just a strategy but a core part of 
Himadri’s identity, shaping its future investments and

world. Himadri is committed to deliver sustainable,

purpose of ‘Together, Towards Tomorrow.’ The Company extends beyond chemistry to build competencies, perspectives 
and partners. 
In line with its ‘Together, Towards Tomorrow’ commitment, Himadri has embedded Environmental, Social, and Governance 
(ESG) principles into its business model. This model outlines ambitious goals that focus on reducing greenhouse gas 
emissions, conserving natural resources and nurturing social well-being. We are aligning our sustainability ambitions 
based on global and national agendas. 
UNGC: The UNGC alignment empowers the Company to engage with a global 
network of businesses, governments and civil society organisations. In turn, this 
creates onward opportunities for collaboration, innovation and joint development.
UNSDGs: From the business model level, we strive to further 17 UN Sustainable 
Development Goals (UNSDGs). As a future-ready responsible corporate citizen, 
Himadri has established a structured organizational framework to actively pursue 
the attainment of Sustainable Development Goals (SDGs).
Science-Based Targets Initiative (SBTi): This reflects the Company’s proactive 
approach to setting ambitious, science driven targets that support global efforts 
to limit temperature rise and combat climate change. Through science-based 
targets, the Company seeks to ensure that its greenhouse gas reduction strategies 
are enduring, measurable and relevant to the global climate agenda.
Mission LiFE: Himadri also aligns with the Indian Government’s Mission LiFE, a 
nationwide initiative that promotes sustainable lifestyles and reduces activity 
impact on the environment. Mission LiFE encourages citizens, businesses and 
communities to support environmental protection and resource conservation 
through actions.
Global DEI Alliance: This commitment has strengthened the organisational 
framework and helped build a work environment that embraces individuals of all 
backgrounds, identities and experiences. The Company recognises that diversity 
and inclusivity are not just social responsibilities but also business imperatives. 
By aligning with the Global DEI Alliance, it is embedding the principles of 
Diversity, Equity and Inclusion into operations — from recruitment and workforce 
development to leadership, collaboration and innovation. This commitment has 
strengthened its organizational framework, fostering a workplace that values 
diverse backgrounds, identities, and experiences. 
International Council of Chemical Associations (ICCA): During the reporting year, 
Himadri aligned with the Responsible Care® initiative, supported by the Indian 
Chemical Council. This global commitment drives continuous improvement and 
transparent communication in safety, health, and environmental performance. By 
embedding the seven Responsible Care® codes, Himadri goes beyond regulatory 
compliance, implementing proactive measures and innovative practices to uphold 
the highest industry standards. This reinforces its dedication to safety, sustainability, 
and responsible growth.
International Sustainability and Carbon Certification (ISCC): Himadri is 
committed to driving sustainability and advancing its environmental stewardship 
through globally recognized standards. Our adherence to the ISCC underscores 
our dedication to sustainable raw material sourcing, traceability, and reduced 
carbon emissions. By aligning with ISCC protocols, we ensure that our products 
contribute to a circular economy, promoting responsible resource utilization while 
minimizing our environmental footprint. This certification reflects our pledge 
towards sustainable growth and reinforces our commitment to global climate goals

The Company adopted key messages on sustainability to 
drive its global and national agendas.
As a leader in the speciality chemical sector, Himadri 
focuses its sustainability efforts on Planet, People, 
Communities, and Governance. Throughout our journey, 
we continuously innovate and strive to enhance our 
ESG (Environmental, Social, and Governance) initiatives, 
supported by our management and dedicated workforce. 
These efforts have enabled Himadri to gain global 
recognition from EcoVadis, a third-party assessor of 
ESG performance. In our second EcoVadis submission, 
Himadri proudly secure platinum medal, positioning it self 
amongst the top 1% organizations assessed by EcoVadis. 
During 
the 
reporting 
year, 
Himadri 
aligned 
with 
Task Force on Climate-related Financial Disclosures, 
disclosing climate-related information to promote a 
dialogue with investors and other stakeholders. The 
Company participated in its first evaluation by the 
Carbon Disclosure Project where we positioned ourselves 
strongly by securing B rating in climate change and water 
stewardship disclosures . 
Himadri’s engagement with British Safety Council helps 
advance workplace health and safety. The esteemed 
British Safety Council provides training, certifications and 
audits to strengthen health and safety protocol. During 
the current reporting year, Himadri has been conferred 
with the prestigious British Safety Council Merit award.
Governance & Ethical Business Practices
Himadri’s Environmental, Social, and Governance (ESG) 
framework is designed to be robust and adaptable, 
enabling the Company to respond proactively to 
global shifts, drive sustainable expansion, and address 
challenges across short-term, mid-term, and long-term 
horizons.
At the core of this ESG agenda is a team of experienced 
committee members who provide strategic oversight 
and data-driven decision-making. The Board of Directors 
plays a pivotal role, overseeing ESG-related risks, 
opportunities, and governance, while the CMD-CEO and 
functional teams take responsibility for on-the-ground 
execution and integration of ESG principles into daily 
operations.
Recognizing climate change as a critical governance 
issue, the Board ensures that climate considerations 
are embedded in the Company’s strategic discussions, 
investment decisions, risk assessments, and performance 
evaluations. Board members bring diverse expertise 
across finance, governance, natural resources, and public 
policy, ensuring a comprehensive and forward-thinking 
approach to sustainability.
Himadri believes that businesses have the power to 
drive lasting social, economic, and environmental 
transformation. Every employee upholds the highest 
standards of integrity, responsibility, and transparency, 
ensuring that sustainability remains a core business 
priority. By embedding ESG stewardship into its 
operations, Himadri advances its sustainable growth 
strategy, ensuring a positive impact on society and 
the 
environment.

The CMD-CEO, as the highest decision-making authority, 
has made it clear that compliance violations must be 
promptly identified, addressed, and met with appropriate 
corrective actions. The ESG Council is responsible for 
upholding Himadri’s values, ensuring that the compliance 
management system remains effective, aligned with 
regulations, and continuously improved.
To mitigate compliance risks—particularly those related 
to 
sustainability, 
anti-bribery, 
corruption, 
and 
fair 
competition—Himadri implements a structured approach 
that includes:
 
 
Regular audits and due diligence across all business 
activities and locations.
 
 
Comprehensive risk analyses conducted by each 
business unit to proactively identify potential 
vulnerabilities.
 
 
Binding standards issued by the ESG Council, 
developed in collaboration with the ESG Committee 
at the Board level.
As compliance landscapes evolve, management bodies 
continually assess significant changes and adjust policies 
accordingly. Periodic risk analyses are conducted in 
critical compliance areas, including anti-corruption, 
antitrust regulations, and money laundering prevention, 
ensuring that Himadri remains a leader in ethical and 
responsible business practices.
By embedding rigorous compliance management into 
its ESG framework, Himadri safeguards its business 
operations, upholds regulatory integrity, and reinforces 
its commitment to sustainable and ethical growth.

Anti-Bribery & Corruption Policy
Himadri’s anti-bribery and corruption framework cultivates 
integrity across business operations. This framework 
provides guidelines for employees, contractors and 
third-party stakeholders to prevent unethical practices 
(bribery, facilitation payments and gifts) that could 
influence business decisions. Some of the key features of 
this policy are:
 
 
Mandatory training and awareness
 
 
Zero tolerance
 
 
Compliance and continuous monitoring
Fair Competition & Ethical Business Conduct
Himadri is dedicated to operating within a fair, 
transparent, and competitive market, fully adhering 
to antitrust and competition laws. This commitment is 
embedded in the Company's governance framework, 
ensuring that all business activities are conducted with 
integrity, accountability, and in compliance with global 
regulatory standards.
The framework encompasses:
 
 
Market compliance
 
 
Fair practices
 
 
Mandatory training and awareness
By integrating these principles, Himadri promotes healthy 
market competition, safeguards stakeholder interests, 
and reinforces its reputation as a responsible corporate 
entity committed to ethical business conduct.
Data Protection and Security Framework
Digital data safety is paramount. Himadri’s data 
protection and security framework is aligned with 
national data privacy regulations, such as the Digital 
Personal Data Protection Act 2023 (DPDPA), ensuring 
that personal and Company data are protected against 
unauthorised access, breaches, or misuse. Key features of 
this frameworks are:
 
 
Data encryption and security protocols
 
 
Data governance
 
 
Mandatory training and awareness
Whistle-blower policy
Himadri’s 
framework 
upholds 
transparency 
and 
accountability by providing employees and stakeholders 
with a secure, confidential, and retaliation-free mechanism 
to report unethical practices. The Company has established 
a structured whistle-blower policy and hotline, allowing 
individuals to report concerns anonymously. To foster a

culture of trust and integrity, Himadri ensures strict non-

employees understand their ethical responsibilities and 
the importance of reporting misconduct. By embedding

Act Responsibly for The Planet
Himadri is focused on reducing its carbon footprint, 
optimizing resource efficiency, and integrating cleaner 
technologies. Deriving from the conducted Corporate 
Sustainability Reporting Directives (CSRD) recommended 
double materiality analysis, Himadri recognises its 
responsibility to minimise its environmental impact. The 
Company has set ambitious targets and implemented 
robust measures to achieve its goals. Key sustainability 
priorities  identified through a comprehensive materiality 
analysis 
include 
climate 
change 
mitigation, 
GHG 
emissions reduction, energy and water management, 
product stewardship, waste management, and circular 
economy promotion. These initiatives are supported 
by an integrated environmental management system 
that complies with legal standards, internal policies, 
and standard operating procedures, ensuring that the 
Company extends beyond compliance to continuously 
improve environmental performance. As a forward-
thinking organisation, Himadri addresses climate change, 
marked by extreme weather events. The Company is 
committed to reduce all climate-relevant emissions and 
minimise the environmental impact of its operations. To 
manage climate-related risks and opportunities across its 
value chain, the Board’s ESG Committee, complemented 
by the Audit Committee and ESG Council, leads efforts to 
address these challenges. At Himadri, addressing climate 
risks is one thing; it is imperative to seize opportunities 
through strategic policies and actions as well. Himadri 
deployed policies addressing key environmental factors 
pertinent to the speciality chemicals sector, aligning  with 
global and national goals. The Company’s environmental 
policies and frameworks are outlined below:

we are dedicated to combating climate change by reducing 
greenhouse gas emissions and achieving net-zero by 2050.
During the reporting year, the company has publicly 
published the net-zero 2050 roadmap. In accordance 
with SBTi guidelines, our net-zero roadmap has been 
clearly distributed into short-term, mid-term, and long-
term business goals and strategies. 
Short-term- The Company aims to achieve climate 
change resilience by incorporating diverse fuels and 
minimizing energy consumption. These are expected to 
reduce carbon footprint at the corporate and product 
levels. The Company is exploring product end-of-life 
recycling initiatives and is committed to reduce emissions 
across the value chain. The Company implemented a 
comprehensive sustainable procurement policy. During 
the reporting year, it launched an outreach programme 
for value chain partners to assess their alignment with 
our sustainability journey. Key initiatives during the short-
term phase are given below:
 
 
Develop a structured climate resilience strategy to 
address identified climate risks.
 
 
Establish mandatory mitigation guidelines for all new 
projects, mergers, and acquisitions, incorporating 
energy efficiency and diversified fuel sources.
 
 
Integrate de-carbonization goals into the annual 
business planning process.
 
 
Embed climate-related KPIs into performance 
evaluations for executives and managers.
 
 
Implement a supplier engagement program to drive 
climate action across the value chain.
 
 
Collaborate with communities to enhance climate 
resilience and integrate adaptation measures into 
CSR initiatives based on identified risks.
 
 
Launch a carbon capture pilot project to explore 
emission reduction opportunities.
 
 
Expand renewable energy adoption wherever feasible.
 
 
Promote a circular economy through recycling and 
resource efficiency initiatives.
 
 
Reduce both upstream and downstream emissions 
to minimize the overall carbon footprint.
Mid-term- The Company is accelerating green initiatives 
to reduce its carbon footprint. In the pursuit of net-zero 
emissions, it plans to integrate feasible and sustainable 
next-generation 
fuels 
into 
operations, 
adopting 
innovative energy solutions that reflect a commitment 
to environmental stewardship. As part of its corporate 
strategy, the Company sets an ambitious goal to electrify 
its entire operation. This transition to electric power is 
intended to significantly reduce its reliance on fossil fuels, 
moderating greenhouse gas emissions. By leveraging 
advanced technologies and renewable energy, it aims to 
make operations efficient and eco-friendly. In this phase, 
the Company will emphasise on emissions reduction 
across the value chain. It recognises that sustainability 
must extend beyond its operations to include its 
suppliers and partners as well. To this end, the Company 
is implementing comprehensive measures to assess and 
mitigate value chain emissions, ensuring that each link in 
its supply chain aligns with environmental goals. Through 
collaboration and innovation, the Company aims to set 
a new sectorial standard for sustainability. Key initiatives 
during this phase are as follows:
 
 
Identify and pilot green business opportunities, 
including energy storage technologies, low-carbon 
footprint grades of carbon black and coal tar pitch.
 
 
Identify specific areas for policy advocacy, such 
as policies aimed at mitigating technological and 
contractual barriers to moving away from coal and 
addressing infrastructural bottlenecks for cleaner 
fuel use.
 
 
Identify 
opportunities 
arising 
from 
the 
implementation of carbon taxes in operations
 
 
Develop a climate-resilient infrastructure.
Long-term- The Company is committed to scaling proven 
technologies and positioning itself as a future-ready 
leader. In this phase, it will integrate next-generation 
technologies across operations, ensuring it remains 
at the forefront of innovation and sustainability. By 
adopting advanced digital tools, automation, and smart 
systems, the Company aims to enhance efficiency, reduce 
environmental impact, and drive sustainable growth. This 
includes the incorporation of renewable geothermal 
energy solutions and energy-efficient technologies to 
lower its carbon footprint. This holistic approach will 
not only make operations more sustainable but also 
resilient to evolving challenges. Himadri’s commitment 
to technological advancement reflects its dedication to 
continuous improvement, environmental responsibility, 
and long-term stakeholder value, strengthening its global 
competitiveness. Some of the key initiatives during this 
time frame are given below:
 
 
Update the Net Zero plan, taking into consideration 
new 
regulatory, 
market 
requirements 
and 
achievements with short to medium-term targets.
 
 
Develop and implement a Just Transition plan.
 
 
Scale the use of renewable fuels and energy for 
transportation.
 
 
Initiate the consumption of renewable geo-thermal 
energy.
 
 
Integrate carbon capture across all business units.

of the Board's Report (Contd.)

198
Group level objectives/KPIs to drive our Net-Zero 2050 
vision are
 
 
Reduce energy intensity/Mt of product sold by 10% 
by 2025 against baseline (2021)
 
 
Reduce Scope 1&2 CO2e emission intensity/Mt of 
product sold by 25% by 2025 against baseline (2021)
 
 
Reduce Scope 3 CO2e emission intensity/Mt of 
product sold by 5% by 2025 against baseline (2023)
Apart from the regulatory requirement, Himadri always 
recalibrate its efforts to push further its ambitions once 
a landmark is achieved. During the reporting year, all our 
group level targets are achieved with help of strategic 
guidance from the leadership and efforts made by our 
employees and workers .
As mandated by our comprehensive Energy Management 
framework, energy audit is to be conducted in every three 
years by engaging independent external third party. 
Additionally, our in house energy managers regularly 
conduct energy review as per instructions from Bureau of 
Energy Efficiency (BEE), Government of India. Moreover, 
GHG calculations/ Carbon accounting takes place every 
year by engaging external third party and internal team. 
GHG accounting data are subsequently verified by 
another independent third party verifier.
Aligning with the outcome of energy audit, we have 
begun implementation of digital energy management 
system at Carbon Black Division, Mahistikry location. We 
have installed Smart Comm software by L&T Electrical 
and Automation for energy management system. In 
Carbon Black Division, new smart meters are installed in 
generating unit and different Process distribution section 
and sub section to monitor auxiliary power consumption 
trend in different sections. Specific energy consumptions 
at different processes and sections can be easily analysed 
with the installed system.
Himadri has replaced the conventional fuel oil heating 
system with a steam heating system in its new 480Ton per 
day Coal Tar Distillation project. By switching to steam 
energy, the company benefits from improved heating 
performance, potentially lower energy costs, reduced 
GHG emissions, lower maintenance requirements.
Himadri has undertaken strategic initiatives to reduce 
energy 
consumption 
by 
implementing 
sustainable 
solutions across its operations.
Glimpse of capex undertaken in FY 24-25 to 
advance environmental stewardship
Reclaiming Waste Heat from Line #3 Secondary APH:
Previously, hot air (around 350°C) from our Line #3 
process was being released into the atmosphere. 
This waste heat stored valuable energy that could 
support our boiler operations. Following energy audit 
recommendations, we installed a duct to redirect this hot 
air into Boiler #3. This reduced the reliance on ambient 
air (~30°C), improving boiler efficiency and reducing fuel 
consumption. Steam generation increased from 69.14 to 
73.86 TPH using the same amount of fuel. The use of hot 
air also replaced diesel during maintenance and lowered 
the power demand of the fans. This initiative saved over 
9,559 MWh of energy annually and cut approximately 
4,588 tons of CO2 emissions.
Smarter Control of Boiler Feed Pumps Using VFDs:
Our boiler feed pump was previously delivering more 
pressure than necessary, leading to energy losses. To 
address this, we implemented an advanced control 
system that adjusts pump speed based on real-time 
demand. Variable Frequency Drives (VFDs) were added 
to fine-tune the pump’s output. This optimization reduced 
the discharge pressure from 81 to 75 kg/cm2, bringing it 
closer to the actual requirement. As a result, the system’s 
energy use decreased by 204 MWh per year, and 98 
tons of CO2 emissions were reduced, enhancing both 
efficiency and environmental performance.
Optimizing CO Pump Pressure with Impeller De-staging:
Some of our CO pumps were producing more pressure 
than required, causing unnecessary energy use and

system wear. Instead of installing electronic controls, we 
applied a mechanical solution: removing two impeller 
stages from the pump. This reduced the discharge 
pressure to a more suitable 35 kg/cm2 and eliminated 
excess recirculation. The change lowered the pump’s 
energy consumption from 109 to 84 kWh, resulting in 
annual energy savings of 213 MWh and a CO2 emissions 
reduction of about 102 tons.
Sealing Leaks in the Compressed Air System:
A detailed survey revealed that 12.5% of our compressed air 
was being lost through undetected leaks. Using ultrasonic 
equipment, we identified and sealed these leaks, reducing 
overall air loss to 9.8%. This action recovered around 202.7 
CMH of compressed air and improved system efficiency. 
The improvement translated into an annual energy saving 
of 177.6 MWh and a reduction of 85 tons of CO2 emissions. 
This simple yet effective measure helped optimize one of 
our most energy-intensive utilities.
Installing Zero-Loss Drains in the Compressed Air 
System:
Earlier our air drainage system operated on a timer, 
releasing compressed air every minute regardless of 
actual need. This led to continuous loss of air and energy. 
We replaced these with zero-loss drains that only activate 
when moisture is present. This upgrade was implemented 
on both the 6-bar and 12-bar compressor lines. Together, 
the systems saved 320 MWh of energy per year and 
reduced 147 tons of CO2 emissions, all through a simple 
automation improvement.
Water Management
Himadri continues to focus on established water 
management initiatives, including monitoring water 
stress levels across relevant sites. Adequate water 
availability for cooling and production processes is 
essential. Himadri implemented regular analyses of short, 
medium and long-term water risks across sites. During 
the reporting period, Himadri widened its water stress 
assessments to encompass a comprehensive evaluation 
of water related risks. Himadri is committed to sustainable 
water management, adopting advanced technologies 
and practices to reduce freshwater consumption, recycle 
wastewater and mitigate environmental impact. 
Water risk analysis and reduction goals: Himadri utilises 
the WRI Aqueduct tool to analyse physical risks such as 
water stress, flooding and water quality. The Company 
conducts water risk assessments based on water basins 
and site-specific water use. With a goal to reduce specific 
freshwater intake by 20% relative to production volume 
between 2021 and 2026, Himadri has implemented 
various measures across its production sites.  All Himadri 
plants employ Zero Liquid Discharge (ZLD) technology 
through an Effluent Treatment Plant (ETP) integrated 
with a Water Recovery Plant (WRP). This system ensures 
wastewater recycling and efficient reuse, significantly 
reducing groundwater consumption. 
We also aim at enhancing water efficiency, by adhering 
to the National Action Plan on Climate Change (NAPCC)
with advanced water-saving technologies for improved 
water management. We will align with the National 
Water Mission by monitoring and minimizing water 
withdrawal and consumption. Additionally, the purpose 
of this framework is to outline the procedures and 
responsibilities for monitoring and managing waste water 
quality at Himadri. The objectives are to: 
 
 
Achieve and exceed Zero Liquid Discharge (ZLD) 
objectives. 
 
 
Reduce the intensity of fresh ground water 
withdrawal by 20% by 2026 against baseline (2021). 
 
 
Reduce daily water consumption by 20% by 2026 
against baseline (2021)
 
 
Enhance capabilities to recycle and repurpose water 
resources, ensuring a minimal ecological footprint. 
 
 
Maintain consistent and transparent disclosure 
of advancements to uphold accountability and 
stakeholder 
trust. 
Himadri 
is 
committed 
to 
environmental 
sustainability 
with 
Zero 
Liquid 
Discharge (ZLD) through the comprehensive reuse 
of wastewater from our processes. Our advanced 
Effluent Treatment Plant (ETP) and Water Recovery 
Plant (WRP) are pivotal in this endeavor.
As mandated by our comprehensive Water Management 
framework, water audit including water withdrawal, water 
consumption and waste, is to be conducted in every three 
years by engaging independent external third party. 
Additionally, our in house internal auditors regularly 
conduct water withdrawal and consumption review as 
per instructions from Ministry of Jalshakti, Government 
of India. Moreover, water conservation projects and their 
impact is monitored every year by engaging external 
third party and internal team. Water management data 
are subsequently verified by another independent third 
party verifier.
At Himadri, we have implemented an efficient condensate 
recovery system, which enables operation to recover 60% 
of the low-pressure (LP) steam used in all equipment, 
line tracing and coils. Through an efficient vapour trap 
system, we condense water from LP vapour, effectively 
reducing our groundwater usage.

Responsible Consumption
Himadri’s efforts to reduce production waste are guided 
by a principle: Avoid Waste. If avoidance is not possible, 
waste should be recycled or used in energy generation. 
If recycling or energy generation is not feasible, waste 
should be disposed safely. The need to establish high-
level circular economies that support sustainable 
economic growth is increasingly critical. Given the 
planet’s finite resources, rising lifestyle standards and 
growing resources demand on account of a rising global 
population, conventional one-way economic models will 
no longer be able to sustain prosperous lifestyles and 
cultures going ahead. To stimulate economic activity and 
move to a decarbonised society, it will be essential to 
reduce the use of fossil-based plastics while addressing 
a growing demand for plastics. In this context, Himadri 
acknowledges the growing importance of reducing 
plastic consumption and enhancing recycling. In addition 
to plastics and hazardous waste, Himadri’s waste 
management initiatives encompass a wide range of Key 
Performance Indicators (detailed below).
 
 
Achieve <1% waste to landfill intensity by 2026 
against baseline (2021)
 
 
Increase the use of non- virgin raw materials sourced 
externally to over 95% in production processes
 
 
Ensure 100% compliance with regulators
Process optimisation is central to Himadri. This includes 
processing of substance streams and the application of 
the 3R principle (reduce, reuse, recycle) across operational 
sites. Where waste cannot be avoided, the focus is 
on mechanical or thermal reprocessing. At Himadri’s 
sites, various types of recyclable waste — plastics, 
glass, paper, food waste, and wood—are segregated 
and dispatched to external recycling firms approved by 
regional pollution control boards. The Company monitors 
Water Intensity 
these firms through audits to ensure their corresponding 
compliance with statutory provisions. Himadri adheres 
to the recommendations of state government waste 
management authorities related to handling hazardous 
wastes like effluent sludge, oil-contaminated gloves, jute 
and soak sand. It employs vendors authorised by the 
pollution control boards. The Company reintroduced 
recycled products as inputs following the end-of-life 
phase of its products. Himadri leverages the benefit of 
integrated production sites and systems for systematic 
waste management. Byproducts from one production 
process are repurposed as raw materials of other 
products, widening the value chain. The Company sources 
raw materials from other sectorial by-products (coal tar 
and carbon black feedstock). In addition to reprocessing, 
waste with high calorific value (substitute fuel) is used 
to produce energy, reducing a reliance on primary fossil 
fuels and moderating Company’s carbon footprint.
In the context of a circular economy, using Anthracene 
oil derived from coal tar as a feedstock for carbon black 
production is an innovative and sustainable approach 
that significantly contributes to resource efficiency and 
environmental sustainability. Coal tar, a by-product of 
coal processing, contains a variety of valuable chemical 
compounds, 
including 
Anthracene 
oil. 
Traditionally, 
Anthracene oil had Limited scope industrially or got 
disposed of, contributing to environmental pollution. By 
redirecting Anthracene oil into the carbon black production 
process, Himadri is not only creating a valuable industrial 
product but also closing the loop in the life cycle of coal 
tar derivatives, ensuring that fewer resources go to waste. 
Additionally, the circularity of this process is critical for 
minimizing the carbon footprint of the carbon black 
industry. By integrating the use of a by-product into the 
production process, total emission reduction is achieved by 
45% compared to Anthracene Oil disposal and combustion.

partners, and society. By integrating sustainability across 
our operations, we strive to uplift, empower, and enrich 
the lives of those who contribute to and benefit from our 
value chain.
Occupational Health and Safety (OHS) is at the heart 
of our corporate framework and an essential pillar of 
our workplace culture. Our unwavering commitment is 
to ensure that every individual—whether an employee, 
contractor, or business partner—returns home safely 
each 
day. 
By 
prioritizing 
safety, 
well-being, 
and 
professional development, we are building a workplace 
where people thrive, businesses grow, and communities 
prosper—together. The Company’s occupational health 
and safety vision Zero Accident/Incident is grounded in 
a proactive framework focused on four pillars - Learning, 
Culture, Commitment and Communication. This vision is 
dedicated to create a safe, healthy work environment. By 
implementing comprehensive safety measures, proactive 
risk management and continuous training, the vision 
strives to eliminate workplace accidents and incidents. 
This commitment promotes care, accountability and 
excellence in health and safety practices, ensuring that 
every individual returns home safely from work.
Himadri’s journey from traditional safety approaches 
to Vision Zero Incident/ Accident philosophy focuses 
on specific targets to prevent accidents, while Vision 
Zero views safety as an integral journey and part of the 
business Traditional safety management often comprises 
programmes led by designated individuals and measures 
performance through injury benchmarks. In Order 
to achieve what we aspire for, Himadri establishes 
comprehensive occupational health and safety policies 
and frameworks with clear Objectives as shown below.

Occupational Health & Safety
At Himadri, occupational health and safety (OHS) is a top 
priority, embedded in every aspect of our operations. Our 
proactive and structured approach ensures a safe and 
secure workplace, fostering a culture where employee 
well-being is paramount.
Our OHS management system is built on a comprehensive 
risk assessment framework, enabling us to identify, 
evaluate, and mitigate potential safety hazards before 
they pose a risk. By conducting detailed risk profiling, 
we proactively implement preventive and corrective 
measures, minimizing workplace incidents and ensuring 
operational continuity.
Himadri’s OHS framework is fully aligned with global 
industry standards, including ISO 45001 (Occupational 
Health and Safety Management) and SA 8000 (Social 
Accountability). 
This 
structured, 
industry-compliant 
approach not only safeguards our employees but 
also extends to third-party contractors, visitors, and 
stakeholders across our operations.
Through continuous training, monitoring, and adherence 
to best practices, we reinforce a safety-first culture, 
ensuring that every individual in our workplace feels 
protected, valued, and empowered to contribute to a 
healthy and resilient work environment.

Himadri’s occupational health strategy focuses on a cycle 
of strategies to ensure a safe and supportive workplace. 
These include Risk Assessment, Standardization of 
Procedures, Workplace Health, Training on Occupational 
Health, 
Management 
of 
Occupational 
Hygiene, 
Occupational 
Health 
Services, 
Rehabilitation 
and 
Institutional Support for work-related injuries or illnesses, 
Internal/External Audits and Continual Improvement. 
The focus is on identifying potential hazards, evaluating 
risks, creating consistent safety protocols, promoting 
physical and mental well-being, maintaining hygiene 
standards, providing medical support and providing 
rehabilitation and institutional support for employees. 
Risk assessment is essential for identifying, evaluating 
and mitigating workplace hazards to protect employee 
safety and wellbeing. Himadri follows a general Risk 
Assessment, categorizing risks into high, medium, and 
low levels. High and medium risks are reviewed monthly 
by Top Management at the ESG council level. At Himadri 
we have established Occupational Health Centre (OHC) 
to take care the Medical issues of employee and workers 
(including third party). Additionally, being a speciality 
chemical 
manufacturer, 
Himadri 
has 
implemented 
proactive measures for the safe and secure handling of 
hazardous chemicals through a structured framework. 
Himadri has developed a comprehensive standard 
that outlines the procedures for handling, storage and 
disposal of hazardous chemicals to prevent accidents 
and exposure. Regular training sessions for employees 
and workers are organized in alignment the SDS 
instructions in accordance with the Globally Harmonized 
System. Additionally, we are providing specific PPEs for 
mitigating the risk of chemical exposures to our front-line 
workforce.
Himadri’s health and safety policy has been carefully 
developed and extended to cover not only employees 
but also all non-employee workmen, such as contractors, 
temporary staff and external labors. This means that 
the safety protocols, risk management procedures and 
standards that apply to regular employees have also 
been communicated(percolated) and enforced for non-
employee workmen working on Himadri’s premises. By 
doing so, Himadri ensures that all individuals regardless 
of their employment status are equally protected from 
occupational hazards and receive the necessary safety 
training and are provided with the appropriate equipment 
and guidance to maintain a safe working environment. 
This is in line with their broader commitment to health 
and safety standards ensuring compliance and a safe 
work culture at workplace. Moreover, Himadri has 
implemented a comprehensive and robust framework to 
ensure the health and safety of non-employee workers 
on its premises. This framework is designed to protect all 
individuals, including contractors, vendors and temporary 
workers by adhering to stringent safety standards and 
ensuring these individuals are fully trained in applicable 
protocols.

Community Engagement & CSR Impact
Himadri’s commitment to Corporate Social Responsibility 
(CSR) extends far beyond regulatory compliance—it 
is a core part of the Company’s identity. With a legacy 
spanning over three decades, Himadri has consistently 
championed positive social change, particularly in rural 
and underserved regions. The Company serves as a 
catalyst for transformation, implementing initiatives in 
rural development, healthcare, education, environmental 
conservation, and social empowerment. Each of these 
efforts is driven by the belief that true corporate 
responsibility lies in fostering self-sufficiency, resilience, 
and long-term progress.
Himadri’s CSR initiatives are structured for maximum 
impact under the guidance of its CSR Committee, a 
dedicated Board-level body ensuring that every project 
aligns with the Company’s core values, sustainability 
objectives, and long-term community development 
goals. 
By 
prioritizing 
high-impact 
initiatives, 
the 
Company actively contributes to the United Nations 
Sustainable Development Goals (UNSDGs), reinforcing its 
commitment to global sustainability standards.
Himadri follows a well-defined and structured approach 
to CSR, ensuring that every project is meticulously 
planned, implemented, and monitored from inception to 
completion. The dedicated CSR team ensures optimal 
resource utilization, maintaining the highest standards of 
transparency, accountability, and effectiveness.
To measure the tangible impact of its CSR programs, 
Himadri conducts rigorous assessments, beginning with 
internal evaluations, followed by third-party verifications. 
This dual-layer evaluation enhances the credibility of the 
Company’s efforts, ensuring that every initiative delivers 
measurable and lasting benefits to the communities it 
serves.

CSR

to

Sustainable Value Chain
Himadri plays a vital role in shaping both environmental 
and social outcomes through its extensive global market 
presence. By collaborating closely with value chain 
partners, the Company is committed to preventing human 
rights violations and environmental breaches while 
fostering transparency and traceability across its entire 
supply chain. This commitment is deeply embedded 
in Himadri’s corporate philosophy, Together Towards 
Tomorrow, which underscores a collective and forward-
thinking approach to sustainability.
A strong advocate of circularity, Himadri has developed 
its value chain by upcycling by-products from industries 
such as steel and oil & gas. In its carbon black division, 
the Company harnesses process waste gas to generate 
electricity, a portion of which is used internally, while 
the surplus is exported to the grid—contributing to 
the replacement of coal-generated thermal power. By 
extending product lifecycle phases and embedding 
circular economy principles, Himadri has built a legacy of 
responsible manufacturing.
Supplier selection is another critical aspect of Himadri’s 
sustainability strategy. The Company not only ensures 
that suppliers meet high sustainability standards but 
also enhances the overall resilience and quality of 
the value chain. As a responsible speciality chemical 
company, Himadri acknowledges its duty to minimize 
environmental and social impacts. To achieve this, it has 
set ambitious sustainability targets and implemented 
stringent measures. Through a comprehensive materiality 
analysis, the Company has identified key focus areas, 
including mitigating climate change, reducing GHG 
emissions, upholding human rights and labor standards, 
and strengthening corporate governance. By integrating 
these priorities into its operations, Himadri continues 
to drive meaningful change, ensuring a sustainable and 
responsible future.
To effectively achieve this, we have developed robust 
management structures and control systems within 
our procurement processes, ensuring transparency and 
alignment with our sustainability goals. By implementing 
rigorous evaluation criteria for our suppliers, conducting 
regular audits, and integrating sustainability metrics into 
our decision-making, we ensure that every procurement 
decision supports our broader ESG objectives. This 
approach enables us to mitigate supply chain risks, 
promote ethical sourcing practices, and drive value 
creation throughout the entire value chain. 
Himadri’s Sustainable Procurement Framework is a 
cornerstone of its commitment to responsible sourcing, 
ethical 
business 
conduct, 
and 
advancing 
global 
sustainability objectives across the value chain. Aligned 
with international sustainability standards and the United 
Nations Sustainable Development Goals (UNSDGs), 
the framework integrates Environmental, Social, and 
Governance (ESG) principles into procurement practices 
to ensure a responsible, transparent, and future-ready 
supply network.

1. 	
Supplier 
Self-Assessment 
Questionnaire: 
The 
sustainable procurement journey begins with a 
Supplier 
Self-Assessment 
Questionnaire 
(SAQ), 
which is designed to assess the supplier’s adherence 
to 
Himadri’s 
sustainability 
expectations. 
This 
comprehensive questionnaire evaluates a supplier’s 
policies, practices, and performance across key 
sustainability dimensions, including:
 
 
Environmental management (e.g., emissions, 
waste, water use)
 
 
Labour and human rights (e.g., fair wages, child 
labour, workplace safety)
 
 
Business ethics (e.g., anti-bribery, data privacy)
 
 
Supply chain practices (e.g., subcontracting, 
traceability)
 
 
Governance and compliance
	
The SAQ enables suppliers to reflect on their 
sustainability maturity while providing Himadri 
with valuable insights into potential ESG risks and 
opportunities for improvement.
2. 	
Third-Party Audit (Online/Offsite): To ensure the 
integrity of the self-assessment process, the SAQ 
is followed by an online or offsite third-party audit. 
These audits are conducted by independent and 
globally recognized verification bodies who assess 
the accuracy of the responses submitted, validate 
documentation, and check compliance with relevant 
laws, industry standards, and Himadri’s Supplier 
Code of Conduct.
3. 	
Composite Risk Rating and Categorization: Based 
on the findings from both the SAQ and the third-
party audit, Himadri develops a composite risk rating 
for each supplier. This rating categorizes suppliers 
into various risk levels—such as low, medium, or 
high—based on their potential ESG risk exposure. 
The objective is to create a transparent view of the 
supplier landscape and prioritize risk mitigation 
efforts accordingly.
4. 	 Active Supplier Engagement and Risk Mitigation: 
Himadri takes a proactive and collaborative approach 
to risk mitigation. For suppliers identified as having 
medium or high-risk exposure, the Company initiates 
targeted engagement strategies that include:
 
 
Capacity building through customized training 
and knowledge-sharing sessions
 
 
Awareness programs to educate suppliers 
on 
sustainability 
expectations, 
compliance 
requirements, and industry best practices
 
 
Collaborative action plans, where necessary, 
are co-developed with suppliers to close ESG 
performance gaps through realistic, time-bound 
improvement measures
 
 
Monitoring and follow-ups to track progress 
and support continuous improvement
	
These efforts are geared towards empowering 
suppliers to enhance their ESG capabilities, align 
with global sustainability goals, and ensure long-
term value creation across the supply chain.
5. 	
Driving Collective Impact: Himadri views suppliers 
as strategic partners in its sustainability mission. 
By embedding ESG performance into procurement 
decisions 
and 
encouraging 
suppliers 
to 
take 
ownership of their sustainability journeys, Himadri 
not only strengthens its own value chain resilience 
but also contributes to broader systemic change.
	
Through its Sustainable Procurement Framework, 
Himadri 
is 
fostering 
a 
responsible 
sourcing 
ecosystem—one 
that 
upholds 
human 
rights, 
promotes environmental stewardship, and builds 
long-term partnerships rooted in shared values and 
mutual growth.
	
Moreover, we actively monitor evolving sustainability 
trends and engage in meaningful dialogues with 
our suppliers and stakeholders. This proactive 
approach allows us to regularly assess and update 
our procurement policies, ensuring they remain 
relevant and impactful. By embracing continuous 
improvement, 
we 
reinforce 
our 
commitment 
to 
maintaining 
high 
standards 
in 
sustainable 
procurement and positively contribute to our 
business ecosystem. Our guiding principles of 
“Integrity, Commitment, Passion, Seamlessness, 
and Speed” are embedded in every aspect of 
our 
procurement 
activities. 
The 
procurement 
functionaries, in collaboration with key stakeholders, 
provide comprehensive guidance on all supply chain 
operations, ensuring that our resource utilisation 
is efficient, sustainable, and fully aligned with our 
organisational vision and mission. By embedding 
these values and principles into our procurement 
strategy, Himadri envisions to gain edges as a leader 
in sustainable practices, setting new benchmarks for 
the industry and paving the way for a responsible, 
resilient, and sustainable supply chain that supports 
our long-term growth and value creation.

Financial Statements
At Himadri, sustainability is a shared commitment, deeply 
embedded in the Company’s operations and extended 
across the entire value chain. Embracing a collaborative 
approach, Himadri actively engages with partners 
to minimize environmental impact while delivering 
sustainable solutions. Recognizing that its direct and 
indirect emissions (Scope 1 and Scope 2) contribute to 
the Scope 3 emissions of its customers, the Company 
continuously works to lower its carbon footprint by 
developing low-emission, customer-centric products. 
This integrated approach reflects Himadri’s dedication 
to not only advancing its own environmental goals 
but also supporting the sustainability ambitions of its 
stakeholders.
As part of its customer decarbonization initiatives, Himadri 
has developed low carbon footprint fuel oil (HLSFO) a 
cleaner and more efficient alternative to conventional 
coal tar used for combustion in furnaces at steel plants. 
This innovative solution significantly reduces greenhouse 
gas (GHG) emissions and enhances operational efficiency 
due to its high calorific value. By reducing overall material 
consumption, HLSFO directly contributes to Sustainable 
Development Goal (SDG) 12: Responsible Consumption 
and Production, underscoring Himadri's commitment to 
resource efficiency.
Himadri's Integrated circular business model for the steel 
sector exemplifies its leadership in sustainable industrial 
practices. The Company sources coal tar from steel 
plants and upgrades it using proprietary technology into 
Coal Tar Pitch, HLSFO, and other high-value by-products. 
Among these, HLSFO is supplied back to the steel plants, 
enabling a closed-loop system that minimizes waste 
and maximizes resource reuse. This model reinforces 
sustainability across the value chain by lowering 
environmental impact, improving material productivity, 
and promoting responsible production.
Through such transformative initiatives, Himadri continues 
to drive measurable environmental progress across its 
operations. By embedding sustainable innovation and a 
customer-focused philosophy at the core of its strategy, 
the Company reaffirms its position as a responsible 
industry leader, committed to long-term value creation 
and environmental stewardship.

Way Forward
As Himadri advances on its journey towards a more 
sustainable and responsible future, it is driving forward 
a suite of transformative and forward-looking initiatives. 
Strategic projects such as Carbon Capture, Utilization 
and Storage (CCUS), fuel diversification, advanced 
energy management systems, and strong commitments 
to Diversity, Equity & Inclusion (DE&I), human rights, 
and STEM education are at the heart of this progress. 
These initiatives not only reflect Himadri’s unwavering 
dedication to environmental and social stewardship but 
also position the Company as a pioneer of purposeful 
growth in the chemical industry.
By embedding sustainability deeper into every aspect of 
its operations, governance, and partnerships, Himadri is 
laying the foundation for long-term value creation—not 
just for its stakeholders, but also for the communities 
it serves and the planet it depends on. These forward-
thinking projects are designed to enhance operational 
resilience, accelerate the transition to a low-carbon 
economy, and empower people through education, 
equity, and innovation.
Looking ahead, Himadri envisions a future where business 
success and sustainability are inseparable. In collaboration 
with value chain partners, policymakers, and civil society, 
the Company is committed to shaping a resilient, inclusive, 
and regenerative future. With bold action, innovation, 
and purpose, Himadri is not just adapting to change—it is 
leading it, ensuring that progress today secures a better 
tomorrow for all.

At Himadri, we deeply value our people as our greatest asset and are committed to creating meaningful impact 
for the communities connected to our business. We believe that true success is not just measured in financial 
growth but also in the value we generate for our employees, partners, and society. We firmly believe in upholding 
Diversity and Inclusion as fundamental aspects of our organizational ethos. We ensure that every individual in 
our organization feels respected and appreciated. Our hiring strategies focus on finding the best people for the 
job who bring diversity of thought, experience, cultures, gender, age, and expertise to enrich the organizational 
culture and add impetus to innovation and sustainable growth. The organization has a zero tolerance policy for any 
kind of discrimination across our operations, be it in our hiring, training, promotion, assessment or remuneration 
on the basis of nationality, race, colour, religion, creed, sexual orientation, gender identity, age and disabilities. 
Gender diversity enhances competitive advantage for us, with a focus on achieving gender parity and inclusivity, 
promoting women’s representation in leadership roles, and prioritizing inclusivity at all organizational levels.

22.	 Turnover rate for permanent employees and workers
	
Himadri successfully reduced the turnover rate of employees through a series of strategic initiatives aimed at 
enhancing employee satisfaction, fostering a positive workplace culture and implementing efficient retention 
programs. We initiated regular feedback sessions and open communication channels between employees and 
management which helped to address issues before they got escalated.  Himadri designs and offers various 
leadership training programmes, coaching and mentorship sessions and personalised career development 
programmes to boost employee morale through PRAGATI programme. Regular rewards, both monetary and non-
monetary were provided, fostering a sense of belonging and appreciation. Additionally, we ensured employees 
could balance their professional and personal lives, reducing burnout and enhancing job satisfaction by offering 
flexible work schedules, remote work options etc. We regularly review and adjust compensation packages to 
ensure they are competitive with industry standards.

* Note: Himadri Speciality Chemical Limited holds 40% paid-up equity share capital of Invati Creations Private Limited (ICPL), this

At Himadri, our core commitment is to uplift 
underserved communities and support their journey 
toward self-reliance. Guided by this purpose, we 
design and implement focused, impactful initiatives 
in the areas of women’s empowerment, healthcare, 
and education. These programmes are thoughtfully 
tailored to address local needs and create meaningful, 
long-lasting change. Oversight for all CSR activities 
rests with the Board-level CSR Committee, which 
ensures strategic alignment with the Company’s 
values and goals. The corporate CSR team provides 
overall coordination, while plant-level CSR teams 
play a crucial role in community engagement and 
issue resolution. We maintain active and ongoing 
dialogue with local communities, either directly 
or through trusted implementing partners. Any 
concerns or grievances raised by stakeholders are 
handled with sensitivity, urgency, and care. These are 
addressed by the plant-level CSR teams, under the 
guidance of the CSR Committee, to ensure timely 
and effective resolution. Through this structured 
and compassionate approach, Himadri continues 
to foster inclusive development and contribute 
meaningfully to building stronger, more resilient 
communities.

VII.	 Transparency and Disclosures Compliances
	
Transparency in Himadri refers to the practice of 
openly sharing information, decisions, processes, 
and policies with stakeholders, including employees, 
customers, shareholders, and the Communities. It 
involves being honest, accountable, and forthcoming 
about the organization's activities and operations. At 
Himadri, addressing grievances as an organization 
involves a structured and proactive approach to 
resolve issues and maintain positive relationships. 
Our Grievance Redressal policy being the backbone 
of transparency, establishes a framework which 
involves:
	
1. 	
Establish Channels for Feedback: Creation of 
multiple channels for expressing grievances, 
such as suggestion boxes, hotlines, online 
forums, or regular town hall meetings. Ensuring 
that these channels are accessible by all 
stakeholders.
	
2. 	
Dedicated 
Grievance 
Handling 
Team: 
Designating a team within the organization 
responsible for managing and addressing 
grievances. Provided them with adequate 
training in conflict resolution, communication 
skills, and cultural sensitivity.
	
3. 	
Listen and Empathize: Actively listen to 
the 
concerns 
and 
grievances 
raised 
by 
stakeholders. Empathize with their perspectives 
and demonstrate genuine concern for their 
wellbeing. 
Avoid 
becoming 
defensive 
or 
dismissive of their grievances.
	
4. 	 Document 
and 
Analyze 
Grievances: 
Systematically 
document 
all 
grievances 
received, including details such as the nature 
of the issue, the individuals involved, and any 
supporting evidence. Analyze the grievances 
to identify common themes, root causes, and 
trends.
	
5. 	
Prioritize Grievances: Prioritize grievances 
based on their severity, impact on stakeholder 
and organizational resources available for 
resolution. Focus on addressing high-priority 
grievances promptly to prevent escalation and 
maintain trust with the stakeholder.
	
6. 
Transparent 
Communication: 
Communicate 
openly and transparently with the stakeholder 
about the organization’s efforts to address 
grievances. Provide regular updates on the 
status of ongoing investigations, resolutions, 
and any changes implemented as a result of 
stakeholder feedback.
	
7. 
Engage 
Stakeholders: 
Engage 
relevant 
stakeholders 
in 
the 
grievance 
resolution 
process. Collaborate with these stakeholders to 
gather additional insights, leverage resources, 
and implement effective solutions.
	
8. 	
Implement Solutions: Develop and implement 
solutions to address identified grievances in a 
timely and effective manner.
	
9. 	 Follow-Up and Monitoring: Following up with 
the concerned person after implementing 
solutions to ensure that the grievances have 
been 
adequately 
addressed. 
Monitor 
the 
effectiveness of implemented solutions and 
be prepared to make adjustments based on 
feedback and changing circumstances.

Himadri has consistently recorded zero complaints from stakeholders on any unethical conduct which is a result 
of our diligent and systematic approach. Himadri has a transparent and secure grievance mechanism that allows 
all stakeholders to report any concerns related to our business conduct. This mechanism includes a toll-free 
number and a dedicated email address. The reporting channels are confidential and each grievance is addressed 
by a dedicated committee that ensures prompt investigation and resolution. Overseen by the Chief Sustainability 
Officer, Company Secretary and Chief Human Resources Officer, the system ensures timely and appropriate 
responses to complaints based on their severity. We ensured regular audits, monitoring mechanism, continuous 
and open communication, feedback sessions with all relevant stakeholders.

26. 	 Overview of the entity’s material responsible business conduct issues
	
Our Sustainability initiative focuses on addressing the most significant sustainability challenges and opportunities. 
Himadri has restructured its material topics and adopted the Corporate Sustainability Reporting Directive’s double 
materiality assessment. This methodology prioritizes issues based on their impact on the environment, society and 
Himadri’s business, creating financial risks and opportunities. On one hand, organisations must have an impact 
on people and the environment (inside-out). On the other hand, sustainability-related developments and events 
create (new) risks and opportunities for organisations (outside-in).
	
10. 	 Continuous Improvement: Continuously evaluate and improve the organization’s grievance handling processes 
based on lessons learnt and feedback received. Strive to build trust and foster positive relationships through 
ongoing engagement and responsiveness to concerns.

Health & Safety
Opportunity
Aligned with our core 
business values, beliefs, 
and practices, ensuring 
the safety and well-being 
of our employees is 
paramount. We dedicate 
significant efforts to 
uphold high standards 
of Health, Safety, and 
Environment (HSE) in the 
workplace, recognizing 
that any lapses in these 
areas could have serious 
consequences.
At Himadri, we maintain strict adherence 
to health and safety protocols across 
all our plants and office locations. Our 
commitment to safety is demonstrated 
by our ISO 45001:2018 certification. 
We regularly conduct health and safety 
training for employees and workers, 
supplemented by risk assessment, 
periodic audits and surprise checks to 
ensure full compliance with all protocols.
While an accident may cause 
damage to reputation and incite 
potential legal actions by local 
authority, practicing / delivering 
best in class HSE performance has 
created positive differences to all 
direct and indirect stakeholders 
of the company as well as it 
has enhanced the brand value 
significantly.

Human Rights
Opportunity
A socially responsible 
corporation recognizes 
the importance of 
nurturing strong 
relationships with all 
stakeholders, including 
regulators, investors, 
suppliers, and customers. 
At Himadri by placing a 
high priority on respecting 
human rights, we show 
our dedication to building

with stakeholders and

Himadri is dedicated to sustainable 
development principles, which 
encompass protecting human rights,

As part of this commitment, the Human 
Rights Policy applies to all employees 
and investors, while the Supplier

expectations for our suppliers.
At Himadri, we place a strong

this focus enables us to establish

3
GHG Emissions
Opportunity
Recognizing the adverse 
impact of GHG emissions 
on the global climate, 
we acknowledge this 
as a shared risk. As a 
corporate entity, we are 
fully committed to making 
a positive contribution in 
this regard.
Himadri diligently monitors its Scope 
1 and 2 emissions, striving to enhance 
energy efficiency. The company is 
actively evaluating its emissions and has 
established short-term and long-term 
plans with defined objectives to improve 
energy intensity and reduce its carbon 
footprint.
Additionally, we have initiated 
evaluating our Scope 3 value chain 
emissions which impacts our business 
activities. Subsequently, we will engage 
with relevant stakeholders to mitigate 
Scope 3 emission.
There is an immense positive 
impact of reducing GHG 
emissions, improving energy 
efficiency and air quality, 
eventually contributing to climate 
control initiatives.

Water 
Management
Opportunity
Several processes in 
our operations require 
water. Recognizing 
the significance of this 
finite resource, we are 
committed to reducing 
freshwater usage and 
optimizing our operations.
Himadri has strategically implemented 
Zero Liquid Discharge (ZLD) to 
effectively manage water consumption, 
treatment, and recycling for internal 
use. This initiative aims to continuously 
improve our water consumption 
intensity.
Going beyond commitments, we are 
currently expanding our ZLD plant’s 
capacity to increase water recyclability 
and reusability.
There are many positive financial 
/ non-financial implications 
from reduction in freshwater 
consumption considering quality 
water as a scarce resource.

Enhancing the experience of our

enables us to attain our objectives 
and business performance over 
time.
	
From a broader perspective, double materiality ensures that sustainability reporting focuses on topics that are 
most relevant to the organisation and stakeholders. These material topics upholds the organization’s sustainability 
strategy with the integration of our risk management processes, which consider both immediate risks and long-
term macro trends.

standards applicable across its 
operations. As an integral part of 
employment contracts, it ensures 
all employees understand their

are taken seriously, with potential 
consequences for both the individual 
and the organisation. A Supplier

these standards to business partners, 
establishing binding requirements to 
ensure alignment with Himadri’s ethical 
practices.
The self-declared supplier 
code of conduct mandates 
compliance with Himadri’s 
sustainability standards, including 
environmental protection, labor

and safety. By adhering to this 
code, suppliers contribute directly 
to our broader sustainability 
objectives, fostering a shared 
commitment to responsible

to our robust code of business 
conduct, we ensure economic 
prosperity and societal well-
being for all. Fair competition in 
accordance with free market rules 
lay down equal opportunities 
for all our suppliers enabling 
them to develop product quality 
and transition to a low carbon 
economy.

Digital data safety is paramount. 
Himadri’s data protection and security

data privacy regulations, such as the

2023 (DPDPA), ensuring that personal 
and Company data are protected 
against unauthorised access, breaches, 
or misuse. We ensure Advanced 
technological measures protect 
sensitive data from breaches or 
unauthorised access. Additionally, The 
Company’s robust data governance 
policy ensures a compliance with 
national data protection and privacy 
standards (including Digital Personal 
Data Protection Act 2023).
Himadri ensures responsible and 
secure handling of customer data, 
minimizing the risk of breaches 
and protecting the company 
from legal liabilities and business 
losses. By strengthening data 
security, Himadri enhances

leading to stronger business 
relationships, reduced financial 
risks, and long-term profitability.

 Effective waste

Procurement
Opportunity
By prioritizing ethical 
sourcing and making

socially responsible

Himadri builds strong, 
long-term relationships 
with suppliers who 
share its value. It 
reduces risks associated 
with unethical labor 
practices, environmental 
degradation, and supply 
chain disruptions. By 
prioritizing suppliers who 
adhere to sustainability 
and ethical standards, 
organizations enhance 
reputation, regulatory 
compliance and social 
cum environmental 
outcomes leading to long-
term value creation.
By working closely with our value chain 
partners, we aim to prevent breaches 
of human rights and environmental 
violations. We strive to enhance 
transparency and adequate traceability 
in our value chain entirely. In line with 
the commitment, we have embedded 
‘Together Towards Tomorrow’ in 
corporate philosophy to underline 
our collaborative approach related to 
sustainability endeavors. Value chain is 
a function where although risks exist 
but they are not entirely under Himadri’s 
control. Therefore, we have taken a 
bottom-up approach of identifying 
value chain risks and opportunities not 
only decentralizing the process but 
also encouraging value chain partners 
to seek collaboration. Therefore, we 
have formed a cross functional team. 
The value chain partner engagement 
task force strengthens relationships 
with suppliers, ensuring an alignment 
with sustainability goals (particularly 
in reducing Scope 3 emissions). By 
training and assessing partners’ ESG 
performance, the task force drives 
responsible sourcing practices, 
enhances efficiency and promotes 
sustainability progress across the value 
chain. To ensure that sustainability is 
ingrained throughout our supply chain, 
Himadri employs a multi-stage process 
for selecting and evaluating Supply 
Chain Partners. This process includes:
•	 Non-disclosure agreement
•	 Self-assessment surveys
•	 Composite performance index
•	 On-site and online audits
•	 Collaborative mitigation approach
Sustainable procurement helps 
Himadri reduce costs, mitigate 
supply chain risks, and enhance 
operational efficiency by sourcing 
from environmentally responsible 
and ethical suppliers. It ensures 
resource efficiency, lower 
raw material costs, and waste 
reduction, leading to long-term 
financial savings. Additionally, 
strong ESG-aligned procurement 
attracts investors, enhances 
brand reputation, and secures 
premium market opportunities, 
driving profitability and business 
resilience.

Circular 
Economy
Opportunity
By Adopting circular 
economy strategies 
Himadri showcases its 
potential to transform 
waste management, 
resource efficiency and 
sustainability. By focusing 
on recycling, reusing, and 
waste reduction, a circular 
economy helps moderate 
costs and environmental 
impact. It drives 
innovation in product 
design and business 
models; it enhances 
resource security and 
enhances revenue 
streams, reputation and 
regulatory compliance.
To further our efforts to integrate 
circular economy principles in every 
facets of our organization, Himadri has 
constituted BU level task force. This 
task force drives Himadri’s efforts to 
embed circular economy principles 
throughout the business. By minimizing 
waste, promoting recycling and 
optimizing product lifecycles, this task 
force ensures that resources are used 
efficiently and sustainably. Through 
collaboration across departments and 
initiatives (take-back programmes), 
the task force creates innovation 
and reduces environmental impact, 
contributing to a closed-loop system.
Embracing circular economy 
allows Himadri to maximize 
resource efficiency, reduce waste, 
and create new revenue streams 
by repurposing byproducts and 
extending product life cycles.
•	 Cost Savings – Minimizes raw 
material expenses through 
recycling and waste reduction.
•	 Revenue Growth – Unlocks 
new business opportunities by 
converting waste into valuable 
products.
•	 Regulatory Compliance – 
Avoids fines and benefits from 
government incentives for 
sustainable practices.
•	 Brand & Market Advantage – 
Enhances reputation, attracting 
ESG-focused investors and 
customers willing to pay a 
premium.
•	 Supply Chain Resilience – 
Reduces dependence on finite 
resources, ensuring long-term 
cost stability.
18
Risk 
Management
Opportunity
Effective risk management 
identifies, assesses, 
and mitigates potential 
threats from financial 
uncertainties to 
operational disruptions. 
It ensures regulatory 
compliance, strengthens 
decision-making, 
and protects against 
unforeseen events. By 
proactively addressing 
risks, organizations can 
prevent losses, seize 
opportunities, and deepen 
stakeholder trust.
Himadri has conducted a comprehensive 
risk identification process (as directed 
by the Board). Although the Risk 
Management Committee is expected 
to take the lead in this effort, cross-
committee and common risks are 
being addressed in collaboration with 
other committees mandated by the 
Board. Besides, Himadri incorporated 
sustainability related risks, including 
responses to non-conformities, 
reputational risks and actions that 
could affect the Company’s brand. 
Himadri’s governance risk management 
employs decentralised controls to 
capture granular risks (including 
physical and transition risks). Executives 
are appointed at the operating 
business and group levels to ensure 
comprehensive risk management. 
At the group level, risk registers 
are aggregated to identify material 
risks across three factors: frequency, 
potential magnitude and impact. The 
established risk management system 
monitors quantifiable and non-
quantifiable risks for the prevailing 
year and the mid-term period. Risk 
reporting serves as the starting point 
and outcome of Himadri’s continuous 
risk management. Additionally, we have 
established a separate risk management 
committee. This Committee oversees 
risk identification, assessment and 
mitigation that could impact the 
Company. This Committee (Board 
members and senior executives) ensures 
a robust risk management framework 
aligned with industry best practices 
and regulatory requirements. The 
Committee’s responsibilities include 
monitoring the Company’s risk profile, 
reviewing risk management policies and 
ensuring the implementation of effective 
risk mitigation strategies. By conducting 
periodic risk assessments and stress 
tests, the Risk Management Committee 
ensures that threats are proactively 
addressed and goals achieved.
Effective risk management 
strengthens Himadri’s financial 
stability by proactively identifying, 
assessing, and mitigating 
potential threats across 
operations, compliance, and 
market dynamics.
Reduced Financial Losses – 
Minimizes disruptions from market 
volatility, regulatory fines, and 
operational failures.
Lower Insurance & Compliance 
Costs – Ensures adherence to 
laws, reducing penalties and 
insurance premiums.
Business Continuity & Resilience 
– Protects revenue streams by 
preparing for economic shifts, 
supply chain risks, and climate 
impacts.
Stronger Investor Confidence – A 
well-managed risk framework 
attracts long-term investors and 
enhances credit ratings.
Competitive Advantage – Enables 
proactive decision-making, 
ensuring sustained profitability 
and market leadership.

Management
Opportunity
Energy management 
helps reduce operational 
costs, energy

and supply disruptions, 
strengthening long-

moderated environmental 
impact. It ensures 
resilience against energy 
price volatility and supply 
disruptions. Overall,

key to long-term business

supporting the transition 
to a low-carbon economy.
Energy management will remain a 
focus, as Himadri continues to optimise

of ISO 50001 standards and advanced 
monitoring technologies. This initiative 
will be supported by digital solutions, 
allowing for real-time tracking and 
optimisation of energy consumption to

force drives Himadri’s commitment to 
energy efficiency and sustainability. 
Focused on energy-saving opportunities 
and implementing cutting-edge 
technologies, this task force ensures 
the Company minimises energy 
consumption while maintaining 
operational excellence. Regular audits 
and employee awareness campaigns 
enhances energy conservation, reducing 
costs and contributing to a greener 
future for Himadri.
Effective energy management 
helps Himadri reduce costs, 
improve efficiency, and enhance 
sustainability, leading to 
significant financial gains. The 
benefits are as follows:
•	 Lower Operational Costs –

20
Product 
Stewardship
Opportunity
Product stewardship 
ensures responsible 
product lifecycle 
management. This 
comprises products 
designed for durability, 
recyclability, and safe 
disposal, reducing 
waste and resource 
consumption. Effective 
product stewardship 
enhances brand 
reputation and 
compliance with meeting 
the growing demand for 
sustainable products. 
It fosters innovation in 
creating eco-friendly 
solutions, long-term 
business sustainability and 
environmental protection.
Product stewardship involves 
taking responsibility for a product’s 
environmental and social impact 
throughout its life cycle. Himadri can 
leverage this approach to enhance 
sustainability, reduce costs, and 
strengthen market positioning. Our 
key strategies to further product 
stewardship are as follows:
Eco-Design & Sustainable Innovation 
– Develop low-carbon, recyclable, 
or biodegradable products to meet 
growing ESG demands.
Circular Economy Integration – 
Implement closed-loop systems, 
ensuring product materials are 
recovered, reused, or repurposed.
Extended Producer Responsibility (EPR) 
Compliance – Align with regulatory 
requirements by managing end-of-life 
product disposal efficiently.
Downstream Engagement – Collaborate 
with customers and recyclers to ensure 
responsible product use, disposal, and 
recycling.
Transparency & Certifications – Obtain 
eco-labels and third-party sustainability 
certifications to differentiate products in 
the market.
Customer & Market Advantage 
– Position sustainable products 
as premium offerings, attracting 
environmentally conscious buyers and 
investors.
By embracing product stewardship, 
Himadri can enhance brand value, 
reduce regulatory risks, drive innovation, 
and capture new revenue streams, 
ensuring long-term financial and 
environmental sustainability.
Product stewardship not 
only enhances environmental 
responsibility but also delivers 
significant financial advantages by 
optimizing resource use, reducing 
risks, and creating new market 
opportunities.
Key Financial Benefits:
•	 Cost Savings – Using recyclable 
materials and improving 
product efficiency lowers raw 
material and waste disposal 
costs.
•	 Regulatory Compliance & 
Avoided Penalties – Proactively 
managing end-of-life product 
impacts ensures compliance 
with Extended Producer 
Responsibility (EPR) laws, 
avoiding fines and legal risks.
•	 New Revenue Streams – 
Circular economy initiatives, 
such as recycling and product 
repurposing, create additional 
income from recovered 
materials.
•	 Market Differentiation & 
Premium Pricing – Eco-friendly 
and low-carbon products 
attract sustainability-conscious 
consumers, allowing premium 
pricing and a competitive edge.
•	 Investor & Customer Appeal – 
Strong stewardship enhances 
ESG performance, attracting 
green investors and corporate 
buyers looking for responsible 
supply chain partners.
•	 Supply Chain Stability – 
Sustainable material sourcing 
reduces reliance on volatile raw 
material markets, ensuring cost 
predictability and long-term 
savings.

By addressing climate

Climate change affects

to long-term stability 
and environmental

As a forward-thinking organisation, 
Himadri addresses climate change, 
marked by extreme weather events. The 
Company’s comprehensive risk register 
includes climate change risks that 
cover physical and transition risks cum 
opportunities. This holistic approach 
empowers Himadri to proactively 
manage the diverse risks associated 
with climate change. As Himadri 
looks to the future, its commitment 
to addressing climate change will be 
driven by a multi-faceted approach that 
blends innovation with sustainability. 
The Company believes that achieving 
Net-Zero is not merely the end goal; 
instead, it strives to foster a carbon-
negative economy, creating a better 
planet for future generations. In short 
term perspective, The Company aims 
to achieve climate change resilience 
by incorporating diverse fuels and 
minimizing energy consumption.
At Himadri, addressing climate 
risks is one thing; it is imperative 
to seize opportunities through 
strategic policies and actions as 
well.
Himadri deployed policies 
addressing key environmental

chemicals sector, aligning global 
and national goals.

attracts sustainability-focused

higher investor confidence and 
premium market positioning.
