Integrating the principles of the National Guidelines for Responsible Business Conduct into the structures, policies 
and processes ensure that stakeholder interests are integrated into the business fabric. Creating adequate governance 
enables businesses to contribute towards wider development goals.
Himadri’s policy framework enables the Company to hold itself and its value chain partners to the highest standards 
of environmental and social performance by encouraging an open, compliant and transparent work environment. The 
policy framework is enforced into business operations by the Board.

Financial Statements
Himadri’s ISO certifications are a testament to our 
commitment 
to 
globally 
recognized 
management 
standards and operational excellence. They signal 
to 
stakeholders—including 
banks, 
investors, 
and 
customers—that we are a well-structured, reliable, and 
growth-ready organization. Achieving ISO certification 
requires rigorous compliance with defined international 
standards, demonstrating that our processes meet best-
in-class benchmarks for quality and governance.
During the current reporting year, we continued to sustain 
our ISO certifications. The details are described below – 
ISO 9001:2015 certification (Quality)
Himadri operates with a robust ISO 9001:2015 certified 
Quality Management System (QMS), ensuring that its 
products and services consistently meet customer 
and regulatory requirements. The QMS framework 
emphasizes 
continuous 
improvement, 
risk-based 
thinking, and customer satisfaction, which are integral 
to Himadri’s commitment to operational excellence and 
product stewardship.
Through systematic quality audits, process control 
measures, and performance monitoring, the Company 
ensures that each stage of its operations—from raw 
material procurement to final product delivery—adheres 
to stringent quality protocols. The ISO 9001 certification, 
renewed 
through 
external 
validation, 
underscores 
Himadri’s dedication to delivering safe, reliable, and 
sustainable products aligned with global standards.
ISO 14001:2015 certification (Environment)
The 
ISO 
14001 
certification, 
which 
focuses 
on 
Environmental 
Management 
Systems 
(EMS), 
is 
highly significant for Himadri, especially in terms of 
promoting sustainable practices, ensuring compliance 
with environmental regulations, and improving overall 
operational efficiency. ISO 14001 provides a framework 
for Himadri to manage and reduce its environmental 
impact. By identifying and controlling environmental 
risks, such as emissions, waste, water use, and resource 
consumption, Himadri can improve its environmental 
performance. This includes reducing pollution and 
minimizing the ecological footprint of its operations, 
which is particularly important in the chemical industry 
where processes may involve hazardous materials.
ISO 27001: 2013 certification (Information 
Security)
ISO 27001 is the international standard for information 
security management systems (ISMS). Achieving this 
certification ensures that Himadri has robust security 
measures in place to protect its sensitive data, whether 
it’s related to intellectual property, financial information, 
customer data, or employee records. This is crucial in 
today’s digital age where data breaches can result in 
significant financial and reputational damage. ISO 27001 
helps identify potential security risks, vulnerabilities, and 
threats to information. By implementing the necessary 
controls and policies, Himadri can mitigate risks and 
reduce the likelihood of security breaches, cyberattacks, 
or data leaks. It ensures that all aspects of the company’s 
information security are addressed in a systematic and 
proactive manner
ISO 37001: 2016 certification (Anti-bribery)
The ISO 37001 certification, which focuses on Anti-
Bribery Management Systems (ABMS), is important 
for Himadri for several reasons, particularly as it relates 
to enhancing corporate integrity, improving ethical 
business practices, and ensuring compliance with anti-
corruption regulations. Here’s why this certification is 
crucial for Himadri. ISO 37001 provides a framework for 
Himadri to prevent, detect, and respond to bribery risks 
within its operations. This is important in industries like 
chemical, where business dealings may involve suppliers, 
contractors, and government agencies, all of which 
could present potential risks for corrupt practices. The 
certification helps establish clear policies and procedures 
to prevent bribery, ensuring the company operates with 
integrity. ISO 37001 helps improve Himadri’s overall 
corporate governance by establishing transparency and 
accountability in its operations.
ISO 45001: 2018 certification (Health & Safety)
The ISO 45001 certification, which is the international 
standard for Occupational Health and Safety (OHS)
management systems, is highly important for Himadri, 
especially in terms of ensuring the well-being of its 
employees, enhancing safety practices, and complying 
with regulatory requirements. ISO 45001 provides a 
framework for identifying, controlling, and minimizing 
health and safety risks in the workplace. For Himadri, 
this means creating a safer working environment for 
employees, which is especially important in the chemical 
industry where workers are exposed to potentially 
hazardous materials and processes. By implementing 
ISO 45001, Himadri ensures that its operations are 
designed to protect the health and well-being of its 
workforce. One of the key benefits of ISO 45001 is its 
focus on accident and illness prevention. By identifying 
hazards and implementing controls to minimize risks, 
Himadri can significantly reduce workplace accidents, 
injuries, and occupational illnesses. This leads to fewer 
disruptions in operations, lower medical costs, and less 
absenteeism, contributing to a more productive and 
Annexure IX 
of the Board's Report (Contd.)
Annual Report 2024-25
226
healthier workforce. When employees feel safe and 
valued, it boosts their morale and engagement.  
ISO 50001: 2018 certification (Energy management)
The ISO 50001 certification, which focuses on Energy 
Management Systems (EnMS), is important for Himadri 
particularly in enhancing energy efficiency, reducing 
costs, and demonstrating environmental responsibility. 
ISO 50001 provides a systematic approach for Himadri to 
monitor, measure, and optimize energy use. By adopting 
this standard, Himadri can identify areas where energy 
consumption can be reduced without compromising 
production. This leads to improved energy efficiency, 
helping the company use energy more effectively across 
its operations. Energy costs often represent a significant 
portion of operational expenses, particularly in energy-
intensive industries like chemical and manufacturing. ISO 
50001 helps Himadri implement energy-saving practices, 
such as optimizing equipment, improving operational 
procedures, and reducing wasteful energy consumption. 
These measures can directly result in cost savings, 
improving the company’s profitability.
IATF 16949: 2016 QMS for Automotive industry
The IATF 16949 certification is highly important for 
Himadri. The company is involved in manufacturing 
or supplying products to the automotive industry or 
any sector that is part of the automotive supply chain. 
Here’s a detailed explanation of why the IATF 16949 
certification. Himadri manufactures products such as 
speciality chemicals, components, or materials used in 
automotive manufacturing (e.g., lubricants, additives, 
coatings, etc.), The IATF 16949 certification is critical. 
Which is specifically designed for the automotive industry 
to ensure that products consistently meet high-quality 
standards and comply with safety, performance, and 
environmental regulations. For Himadri, this certification 
ensures that its products meet the precise specifications 
required by automotive manufacturers. Automotive OEMs 
(Original Equipment Manufacturers) and Tier 1 suppliers 
often require that their suppliers adhere to IATF 16949 
to ensure compliance with global quality standards. 
For Himadri, achieving this certification ensures that 
its manufacturing processes and products meet the 
specific requirements of the automotive industry, which is 
essential for maintaining existing contracts and securing 
new business opportunities within this sector.
SA8000:2014 certification (Social accountability) 
Achieving this certification demonstrates Himadri’s 
commitment to ethical practices, such as respecting 
labour rights, ensuring a safe work environment, and 
promoting fair wages. This can enhance the company's 
reputation, fostering greater trust with customers, 
investors, and stakeholders. The SA8000 standard 
requires compliance with international labor laws and 
human rights guidelines. For Himadri, this ensures that 
its operations meet recognized ethical standards, which 
is important for reducing legal and reputational risks 
related to labor issues such as child labor, forced labor, 
discrimination, and unsafe working conditions.
ISO 
22301:2019 
certification 
(Business 
Continuity 
Management Systems)- Stage-1
Himadri has successfully completed the Stage 1 audit of 
the Business Continuity Management System (BCMS) 
under ISO 22301, demonstrating its commitment to 
ensuring business resilience and continuity in the face 
of disruptions. The Stage 1 audit involved a thorough 
review of the organization’s preparedness, policies, and 
processes related to business continuity. Himadri is now 
preparing for the Stage 2 audit, scheduled for April 2025, 
which will assess the full implementation and effectiveness 
of the system. This step further strengthens Himadri’s 
ability to maintain operations and recover quickly from 
any unforeseen disruptions, ensuring minimal impact on 
its business activities.
ISO 20400:2017 certification (Sustainable procurement 
practices)
Himadri has adopted the principles of ISO 20400:2017 
– 
Sustainable 
Procurement 
Guidelines 
to 
embed 
environmental, social, and ethical considerations into 
its procurement strategy. Our procurement framework 
ensures that suppliers align with our values on human 
rights, fair labour, ethical conduct, and environmental 
stewardship. This certification reinforces our dedication 
to building a resilient, inclusive, and accountable value 
chain that supports our Net Zero and human rights goals.

7
Statement by director 
responsible for the 
business responsibility 
report, highlighting 
ESG related challenges, 
targets, and 
achievements (listed 
entity has flexibility 
regarding the placement

I am pleased to present Himadri’s Third Buisness Responsibilty and Sustainability 
Report for Financial Year 2024-25, aligned with GRI standards and driven by our 
ESG strategy, “Together Towards Tomorrow.” This approach strengthens stakeholder 
confidence while positioning Himadri as a global leader in sustainability.
At the core of our vision is our commitment to Net Zero by 2050, with SBTi-validated 
targets including a 25% reduction in Scope 1 & 2 emissions intensity and a 5% reduction 
in Scope 3 emissions by 2025. Key initiatives—**waste gas-to-power conversion, 
low-sulphur oils, and circular economy practices—**have already delivered a 36.08% 
reduction in GHG intensity and 99.56% waste recycling.
Our climate resilience strategy, aligned with TCFD, uses scenario analysis to manage 
risks and develop low-carbon products like speciality carbon blacks and silicon-
graphite anodes.
Safety remains a priority with our Zero-Accident Vision, targeting LTIFR below 1 by 
2025 through strict protocols, employee training, and monitoring systems. Similarly, 
human rights and inclusivity guide our business, in line with the UN Global Compact.
Through sustainable procurement, we assess suppliers on emissions, water use, and 
labor rights, ensuring alignment with de-carbonization and circular economy goals.
Himadri’s sustainability journey is about innovation, responsibility, and transparency. 
Together, we are shaping a low-carbon, resilient future for all stakeholders.

8.
Details of the highest 
authority responsible 
for implementation and 
oversight of the Business 
Responsibility policy 
(ies).
At the highest level, the Board of Directors, led by the Chairman cum Managing 
Director & CEO, is primarily responsible for protecting and enhancing shareholder 
value through strategic decision-making. 
The Company’s Board provides a strategic guidance across the Company’s operations, 
ensuring optimal resource utilisation and addressing governance and sustainability. 
The Company’s decisions are aligned with its vision and mission; strategies prioritise 
the best interests of all stakeholders. The Company’s Independent Directors lead 
the Board Committees that implement Board decisions and maintain continuous 
oversight through thorough reviews of policy and procedure implementation.
Himadri’s ESG governance structure comprises experienced committee members. 
The Board oversees the ESG subject, including associated risks and opportunities, 
while the CMD-CEO and other teams are responsible for decisions aligned with 
objectives. The ESG Committee at the Board level is responsible for overseeing all 
sustainability matters.
The ESG Council, chaired by the Chief Sustainability Officer, periodically reviews 
and oversees the implementation of the Company’s Sustainability Policies. Under 
the leadership of the Chief Sustainability Officer, the committee tracks progress, 
provides updates to the board, and monitors key sustainability KPIs.
The ESG Steering Committee, serving as the highest authority at the unit level, 
is tasked with the implementation of ESG initiatives. This team collaborates with 
functional teams, external partners and industry stakeholders to develop roadmaps 
for sustainability endeavours.

Yes, as previously stated, the ESG Committee is a Board Committee responsible for 
making critical decisions regarding ESG issues, identifying risks, and implementing 
mitigation strategies.
Additionally, the ESG Council reviews the Company’s Business Responsibility and 
Sustainability Report and recommends it to the Board for adoption. The committee 
also approves the Company’s Sustainability Report. Under the leadership of the Chief 
Sustainability Officer, the committee tracks progress, provides updates to the board, 
and monitors key sustainability KPIs.

At Himadri, we are committed to upholding the principles of the National Guidelines on Responsible Business 
Conduct (NGRBC). These guidelines provide a framework for ethical and sustainable business practices, aligning 
with our core values and commitment to corporate social responsibility. Our policies are reflected on the following 
domains of ethical and responsible business conducts. Himadri established comprehensive policies and frameworks 
to reinforce ethical practices, legal compliance and safeguard the reputation. These policies and frameworks 
address critical areas like anti-bribery and corruption, fair competition, environmental stewardship, occupational 
health and safety, and whistle-blower mechanisms. The policies that benefit the organisation are following:

4.	
Does the entity have an anti-corruption or anti-
bribery policy? If yes, provide details in brief and if 
available, provide a web-link to the policy.
	
Yes, Himadri is firmly committed to upholding the 
highest standards of ethics and integrity across all 
aspects of its operations. Our comprehensive Anti-
Bribery and Anti-Corruption Policy reflects this 
commitment and is fully aligned with national anti-
corruption laws. It applies to all employees, including 
the Board of Directors, Key Managerial Personnel, 
suppliers, contractors, third-party vendors, and 
other associated stakeholders.
	
The policy clearly outlines prohibited practices, 
robust due diligence protocols for business partners, 
and strong financial controls designed to prevent 
fraud and unethical conduct. It reinforces Himadri’s 
zero-tolerance approach to bribery and corruption, 
fostering a culture of transparency, accountability, 
and responsible business practices.
	
To ensure open and safe communication, a secure 
and 
confidential 
Speak 
Up 
/ 
Whistleblower 
mechanism is in place. Employees and stakeholders 
are encouraged to report concerns or suspected 
misconduct without fear of retaliation, through 
designated channels such as hotlines, email, or web 
portals.
	
Himadri places a strong emphasis on awareness 
and 
education. 
Regular 
training 
sessions 
are 
conducted for employees, business partners, and 
other stakeholders. All new employees undergo 
mandatory training on anti-bribery and corruption 
standards as part of their onboarding.
	
Audit of Control Procedure:
	
To maintain the effectiveness of the policy, periodic 
internal 
audits 
and 
independent 
third-party 
assessments are conducted. These evaluations ensure 
our practices remain aligned with both national and 
international anti-corruption regulations and help 
identify opportunities for continuous improvement.
	
During FY 2024–25 an independent Anti-Bribery 
Due Diligence Assessment was conducted by TUV 
SUD South Asia Pvt Ltd. The assessment covered 
policy 
implementation, 
risk 
evaluation, 
third-
party management, whistleblower protection, and 
employee awareness across multiple sites. Key 
findings confirmed that:
 
 
Himadri maintains a formal, certified ABAC 
policy with clear accountability structures.
 
 
Training programs are conducted regularly, 
covering both new hires and existing employees.
 
 
Anonymous whistleblower channels are in place 
and actively used.
 
 
Periodic risk assessments and due diligence 
procedures are operational across functions 
and geographies.
	
The assessment identified opportunities to further 
enhance third-party training, contract compliance, 
and targeted risk mitigation. Himadri is committed to 
acting on these recommendations and embedding 
ethical governance deeper within its organizational 
fabric.
	
Risk Overview:
	
Bribery and corruption can significantly harm 
the organisation through various forms, Himadri 
identified few risks in its operations
	
Legal penalties and financial losses
	
Reputational damage
	
Operational and regulatory disruptions
	
Misallocation of resources and internal ethical breaches
	
Exposure to blackmail and coercion

Himadri’s Code of Conduct, well-structured policies 
and framework has ensured zero cases of bribery 
and corruption against internal stakeholders over 
last three years including this FY 2024-25. Himadri’s 
Anti- bribery and corruption policy aligned with 
the Prevention of Corruption Act, 1988 (amended 
in 2018) sets clear guidelines prohibiting bribery, 
kickbacks, unethical business practices encouraging 
employees and stakeholders to report unethical 
practices without fear of retaliation. Our due 
diligence on bribery and corruption is assured by 
TUV SUD South Asia Pvt Ltd and other independent 
verification bodies.
	
Himadri’s

training 
and 
awareness 
programs to all stakeholder including BoD, KMP

whistleblower 
mechanism 
through Speak Up, transparent and secure grievance

Himadri’s Perspective on Corporate Compliance 
Disciplinary Action -  
 
 
The Primary goal is to ensure that all employees 
understand and follow the company’s code of 
conduct, policies, and regulatory obligations.
 
 
Disciplinary action, when justified by evidence 
is approached as corrective and educational 
tool rather than a punitive one, with the goal 
of nurturing a culture of responsibility and 
accountability
 
 
When non-compliance is identified, at Himadri 
investigation, documentation, and consultation 
with HR and legal teams are initiated.
 
 
The severity of action depends on the nature 
and frequency of the breach—ranging from 
verbal warnings to termination in extreme cases.
 
 
Consistent 
application 
of 
disciplinary 
procedures to avoid any perception of bias or 
favoritism.
 
 
Communication is key— Ensuring that the 
employee 
understands 
the 
violation, 
the 
expected standards, and the consequences of 
repeated non-compliance.
 
 
Maintaining a clear audit trail of all actions taken 
to ensure traceability and protection for both 
the company and the employee.
 
 
Training and awareness initiatives are rolled 
out post-incident to prevent recurrence and 
address gaps in understanding.

Himadri’s robust governance framework ensures that all business dealings are reviewed and approved through 
transparent and documented processes ensuring strict compliance with the Code of Conduct. The Code 
of Conduct clearly defines acceptable business practices emphasizing that all BoD, KMP must act in the best 
interest of the company without allowing personal or financial interests to influence their professional judgement. 
Regular training sessions to all stakeholders have been instrumental in fostering awareness about identifying and 
addressing potential conflicts of interest. 
	
Himadri’s fair competition policy prohibits all employees to indulge in cartel like behaviour, and ensures compliance 
with anti-trust laws and promotes fair trade practices avoiding any conflicts in accordance with Competition 
Council of India’s guidelines.
	
Himadri’s Gift, Hospitality and Entertainment Policy requires the disclosure of potential conflicts and outline 
procedures for managing them to prevent bias and maintain trust. 
	
Himadri’s Related party transactions policy ensures transparency and fairness in dealings with related entities, 
preventing conflicts of interest. It outlines the approval process for such transactions, ensuring that they are 
conducted at an arm’s length and are in the best interest of the Company and stakeholders.

8.	
Number of days of accounts payables ((Accounts payable *365) / Cost of goods/services procured):
	
Himadri follow, ethical payment practices, avoids any delays that may negatively impact vendors and suppliers, and 
maintain, responsible financial management. We have achieved the reduction in accounts payable days through 
a combination of process optimization, supplier relationship management and efficient cash flow management. 
We optimized our procurement-to-payment cycle by implementing semi-automated invoice processing systems 
through SAP, speeding up the payment approval process. This significantly reduced vendor invoices, ensuring 
faster payments and minimizing outstanding payables. We strengthened our internal financial controls to monitor 
and track accounts payable performance regularly.

At Himadri, all related-party transactions are conducted at arm’s length and in compliance with norms. Regular 
audits and board approvals are at place to monitor and regulate related party dealings. We also ensure that loans 
comply legal and financial guidelines, avoiding preferential treatment. Monitoring mechanism are in place to track 
repayment schedules and outstanding balances to maintain financial integrity. 
	
At Himadri, inclusiveness is a cornerstone of our business philosophy, extending beyond our operations to 
encompass our entire value chain. We firmly believe that supporting women-led businesses, marginalised and 
vulnerable group led enterprises, Micro, Small, and Medium Enterprises (MSMEs), and local communities plays 
a crucial role in fostering economic growth, social equity, and sustainable development. While our core raw 
materials—by-products of large-cap industries like steel and oil & gas—cannot be directly sourced from these 
groups due to the specialised nature of their production, we have proactively aligned our procurement strategy 
to prioritise consumables from these groups wherever possible. This approach enables us to balance operational 
requirements with our commitment to inclusive growth.

2.	
Does the entity have processes in place to avoid/ 
manage conflict of interests involving members of 
the Board? (Yes/No) If Yes, provide details of the 
same. 
	
Yes, Himadri has instituted robust governance 
mechanisms to prevent and manage conflicts 
of interest among Board members, ensuring 
transparency, accountability, and ethical integrity in 
decision-making.
	
All members of the Board, including Independent 
Directors and Senior Management, are bound by 
a comprehensive Code of Conduct. This code, 
approved and periodically revised by the Board, 
provides explicit guidance on expected ethical 
standards, 
responsibilities, 
and 
protocols 
for 
disclosing potential or perceived conflicts of interest.
	
Key Processes and Safeguards:
	
1.	
Disclosure Obligations:
o	
Directors are required to avoid situations where 
personal or financial interests may conflict with 
those of the company.
o	
In cases where such conflicts are unavoidable, 
Directors must formally disclose the matter:
 
 
For Executives: to their immediate superior.
 
 
For Directors: directly to the Board.
	
2.	
Board-Level Oversight:
o	
Disclosed conflicts are addressed and recorded 
in Board meetings.
o	
Independent Directors play a critical role in 
moderating 
and 
arbitrating 
any 
potential 
conflict between management and stakeholder 
interests.
	
3.	
Professional Integrity Standards:
o	
Directors are required to act objectively, 
ethically, and in the company’s best interest, 
refraining from actions that could bring personal 
gain at the company’s expense.
o	
Abuse of position, exploitation of opportunities 
arising from their role, and any form of undue 
influence are strictly prohibited.
	
4.	
Independent Directors' Code:
o	
Independent Directors are required to uphold 
probity, safeguard stakeholder interests, and 
report 
any 
concerns 
regarding 
unethical 
behavior or potential conflicts.
o	
They are expected to remain independent in 
judgment, and report loss of independence, if 
any, to the Board.
	
5.	
Governance Meetings and Evaluations:
o	
At least one exclusive meeting of Independent 
Directors is held annually to evaluate:
 
 
The performance of the Board and 
Chairperson.
 
 
Flow of information from management.
o	
Directors' performance evaluations are used as 
a basis for re-appointment decisions.
	
6.	
Training and Awareness:
o	
Directors are encouraged to undertake regular 
updates 
on 
governance, 
compliance, 
and 
emerging risks, including conflict-of-interest 
management.
	
7.	
Confidentiality and Transparency:
o	
Directors must maintain confidentiality of 
internal deliberations and corporate information, 
disclosing data only under lawful obligation or 
with proper authorization.
	
Through these structured practices, Himadri ensures 
that decisions at the Board level are free from bias, 
rooted in integrity, and aligned with the principles of 
responsible corporate governance. This safeguards 
not only the company’s operations but also the trust 
of investors and other key stakeholders.

At Himadri, innovation is a way of conducting 
business. 
An 
innovation-focused 
strategy 
has 
empowered our research scientists and engineers to 
deploy cutting edge technology to create bespoke 
products and solutions. The Company’s advanced 
laboratories 
have 
been 
accredited 
by 
NABL. 
Our R&D team comprises experienced national 
and international experts collaborating to bring 
fresh perspectives to problem-solving leading to 
leadership. As a sustainability-driven organization, 
Himadri focuses on the research and development 
of process and operations that optimize the 
operational efficiency along with reducing the 
environmental and social impacts of its activities. 
Research and Development forms the cornerstone 
of Himadri’s enduring legacy, driving innovation and 
progress across all facets of the organization. From 
pioneering the upcycling of industrial by-products 
through cutting-edge processes to integrating 
nanotechnology into future-ready product offerings, 
R&D is deeply embedded in our ethos. Himadri is 
steadfastly investing in advanced technologies to 
meet the challenges of tomorrow, ensuring solutions 
that are both impactful and sustainable. The 
Company’s product innovation pipeline is the result of 
proactive research and development. Over time, this 
has yielded decisive efficiency gains, including lower 
product prices, improved quality and superior yields. 
This innovative approach has been manifested in the 
lithium-ion battery materials domain. The Company 
is working on energy consumption and carbon 
footprint moderation through inventive techniques. 
By harmonizing customer-focused quality research 
with a comprehensive analysis of our products’ 
environmental life cycle, Himadri actively contributes 
to SDG 9—fostering innovation, sustainable industrial 
growth, and resilient infrastructure. We harnessed 
R&D tools like pilot reactors and distillation units 
to revolutionize new product development. The 
Company’s value chain has progressively widened 
across the decade through indigenous research, 
marked by a focus on special product profiles. 
Our innovations cater to the growing needs of 
industries such as electric vehicles, energy storage, 
and fast charging systems. By leveraging advanced 
technologies, we aim to enhance energy density, 
efficiency, and cost effectiveness across all our 
solutions. the Company had introduced 15 grades 
in speciality blacks for tyres, fibres, powder, coating 
and other polymer applications. 
2.	
a. 	
Does the entity have procedures in place for 
sustainable sourcing?
	
	
Sustainable procurement serves as one of the 
backbones for ensuring responsible, transparent, 
and strategic business decisions transitioning 
towards low carbon economy. At Himadri, 
sustainable procurement goes beyond just 
purchasing—it encompasses a holistic view of 
resource utilization, supplier engagement, and 
ethical decision-making. It integrates the principles 
of environmental stewardship, social responsibility, 
and economic value creation, ensuring that we 
not only meet our operational needs but do so 
in a manner that contributes positively to society 
and minimizes our environmental footprint. In line 
with our commitment to responsible sourcing, we 
have developed a comprehensive ‘Sustainable 
Procurement Policy’ designed to ensure that 
our suppliers uphold the highest standards 
of 
environmental, 
social, 
and 
governance 
performance, thereby aligning their practices with 
our sustainability goals. to manage risks, enhance 
supplier performance, and drive sustainability 
across the entire supply chain. Towards achieving 
this, Two sets of Frameworks were set up: 
	
	
1. 	
Supplier Code of Conduct requiring all 
suppliers to commit to a mandatory self-
declaration and 
	
	
2. 
Sustainable 
Supply 
Chain 
Framework 
outlining a set of carefully designed Key 
Performance Indicators (KPIs) to measure 
supplier 
sustainability 
performance 
of 
suppliers quantitatively and qualitatively 
and ensure their operational alignment 
with our sustainable goals. 
	
	
	
A comprehensive due diligence program 
of upstream value chain partners was 
conducted by TUV SUD South Asia Pvt Ltd. 
to ensure alignment with our sustainability 
objectives. which ensured all partners 
met the necessary criteria for responsible 
buisness operations.
	
	
Our sustainable procurement framework. 
	
	
To ensure seamless integration of upstream 
supply chain risks into our enterprise risk register, 
Himadri has adopted a strategic categorization 
of procurement activities into three distinct 
elements: raw material, consumables, and services. 
These categories are meticulously mapped and 
managed according to the ISO 20400:2017 
Sustainable 
Procurement 
Framework, 
which 
serves as a comprehensive guideline to identify 
and address risks, set performance standards, and 
ensure responsible procurement practice.
	
	
https://www.himadri.com/pdf/Sustainable__
Procurement__Policy.pdf

sustainably.

3.	
Describe the processes in place to safely reclaim your products for reusing, recycling and disposing at the end 
of life, for (a) Plastics (including packaging) (b) E-waste (c) Hazardous waste and (d) other waste.
	
As Himadri supplies its products as intermediary raw materials to businesses for manufacturing their end products, 
our products cannot be reclaimed from the customers. However, the company has undertaken a pilot project to 
reclaim carbon black from used tyres and introducing the same in our value chain.
	
Additionally, we are committed to researching and developing sustainable packaging options that are suitable for 
our product to support our sustainability goals.

In line with our commitment to advance environmental stewardship and minimise the carbon footprint, Himadri 
conducted a comprehensive life cycle assessment of key products. These assessments were carried out according 
to ISO 14044:2018, a standard providing a framework that comprises goal definition, inventory analysis, impact 
assessment and interpretation, ensuring that the LCA results are consistently reliable. Conducting an LCA draws 
several values at critical areas from planning, execution and decision making. The LCA covered all critical stages 
of the product lifecycle - from the upstream transportation of raw materials, through the production process, to 
downstream transportation to end-users. The LCA insights enable Himadri to make informed decisions regarding 
raw material sourcing, production efficiency and logistics This approach ensured that Himadri can assess holistic 
environmental impact and identify potential improvement areas.

Process optimisation is central to Himadri. Himadri has initiated to introduce recycled products as inputs following 
the end-of-life phase of its products. Additionally, we have launched a pilot project to implement a reusable 
packaging solution, with the potential to eliminate plastics and wood from packaging. Himadri leverages the benefit 
of integrated production sites and systems for systematic waste management. By-products from one production 
process are repurposed as raw materials of other products, widening the value chain. The Company sources raw 
materials from other sectorial by-products (coal tar and carbon black feedstock) resulting into majority of non-
virgin materials in our value chain.

We are dedicated to advancing our environmental protection initiatives. To turn our commitment into action, we 
have initiated a pilot project to create and apply a reusable packaging solution that could remove plastics and wood 
from our packaging. Guided by the UNSDGs, which serve as a fundamental framework for our daily operations, 
we aim to promote "Responsible Consumption" and a circular economy within our operations and throughout our 
value chain. Consequently, we are exploring various alternative materials to replace plastic packaging. Additionally, 
in alignment with our net-zero roadmap, we aim to eradicate the use of virgin plastic from our operations.

Circularity at Himadri is driven both by environmental and ethical aspects. And our value chain partners epitomises 
this principle. Himadri launched a pilot project to implement a reusable packaging solution, with the potential 
to eliminate plastics and wood from its packaging. Besides, the Company strives to achieve its ambitious waste 
management target (zero waste to landfill). Himadri leverages the benefit of integrated production sites and 
systems for systematic waste management. By-products from one production process are repurposed as raw 
materials of other products, widening the value chain. Himadri follows EPR practices by taking responsibility for 
the entire lifecycle of products, including the collection, recycling and disposal of packaging waste. Himadri is 
advancing tire recycling projects to convert waste tires into reclaimed rubber, recovered carbon black, low sulphur 
industrial oil, and reclaimed steel. This process reduces landfill waste and promotes sustainable material recovery. 
Himadri maintains regular communication with third-party vendors to monitor the final disposal and ensure proper 
management of the waste, reaffirming its commitment to environmental responsibility.
	
Product End-of-Life Management:
	
As part of Himadri’s ongoing commitment to environmental stewardship and circular economy principles, we 
are initiating a comprehensive Product End-of-Life Management Action Plan. This upcoming initiative aims to 
responsibly manage the lifecycle of Himadri’s products beyond their useful phase, ensuring minimal environmental 
impact and enhanced resource recovery.

Principle 3
Businesses should respect and promote the well-being of all employees, 
including those in their value chains.
SDGs Impacted
Sustainable businesses must treat employees and workers within their 
organisation and value chains equitably and with dignity and protect 
their health and safety. Empowering policies, processes and systems 
spanning the employee life cycle ensure equal opportunity, fair 
working conditions and pay, and career development and progression 
opportunities for overall employee well-being.
Himadri operates in a sector where health & safety, employee rights 
and workforce development are essential for operational efficiency. 
Investing in employee development, fair wages and inclusive work 
policies enhances productivity, job satisfaction and retention, 
ensuring a motivated and skilled workforce. Our commitment to 
ethical procurement, fair payment terms and responsible sourcing 
fosters long term partnerships with suppliers and value chain 
partners. Our diverse and inclusive workforce improves decision-
making, innovation and collaboration, making us a more resilient and 
competitive Organization.

At Himadri, we believe that the well-being of 
our employees is the foundation of a thriving, 
engaged, and high-performing workforce. We 
are committed to fostering a work environment 
where 
every 
individual 
feels 
supported—
physically, mentally, and emotionally. Our 
employee well-being initiatives are thoughtfully 
designed 
to 
enhance 
satisfaction, 
boost 
productivity, and promote long-term success 
for both individuals and the organization.
	
Work-Life Balance:
	
	
We 
actively 
promote 
work-life 
balance, 
understanding 
that 
a 
healthy 
equilibrium 
between personal and professional life is key 
to sustained well-being. Through flexible work 
arrangements—including remote work options 
and adaptable scheduling—we empower our 
employees to manage their responsibilities with 
greater ease and confidence.
	
Physical Health:
	
	
Himadri is dedicated to maintaining a healthy 
workplace. We provide ergonomic workstations, 
encourage regular breaks, and offer access to 
wellness programs. Nutritious meals are also 
made available in our canteens, ensuring our 
employees have the fuel they need to stay 
energized throughout the day.
	
Mental Health:
	
	
Our culture is built on openness and support, 
where employees feel safe to discuss mental 
health challenges. We offer access to counselling 
services, 
conduct 
stress 
management 
workshops, and actively create an environment 
that prioritizes psychological safety.
	
	
We also extend our care beyond the workplace. 
In addition to ensuring safe working conditions 
and the prevention of occupational illnesses, 
we organize regular health check-ups for 
employees, workers, and, in some cases, their 
families. Our comprehensive approach to well-
being reflects Himadri’s belief that when our 
people thrive, our business flourishes.

At Himadri, the well-being of workers and employees is not just a responsibility—it is a core principle deeply 
embedded in the company’s values and operational ethos. Recognizing that a healthy, secure, and supported 
workforce is vital for sustainable growth and productivity, Himadri has implemented a comprehensive set of 
welfare measures that holistically address the physical, emotional, and social needs of its people. Himadri’s 
well-being framework rests on several foundational pillars:
 
 
Health Insurance: Himadri ensures that employees and their families have access to quality healthcare 
services through robust health insurance coverage, offering peace of mind in times of medical need.
 
 
Accident Insurance: Understanding the inherent risks in industrial operations, Himadri provides accident 
insurance to safeguard workers against unforeseen workplace incidents, ensuring financial protection 
and quick recovery support.
 
 
Maternity and Paternity Benefits: The company supports its employees through the different phases of 
parenthood by offering maternity and paternity benefits, reinforcing its belief in a family-friendly work 
environment and gender inclusivity.
 
 
Day-care Facility: To further support working parents, Himadri provides accessible and safe day-
care facilities, enabling employees to balance work commitments with family responsibilities without 
compromise.
 
 
Occupational and Non-occupational Health and Safety Support: Himadri goes beyond compliance by 
offering a comprehensive occupational health and safety system. Regular health checkups, safety drills, 
and wellness programs form part of a proactive approach to maintaining a safe and healthy workplace.
	
	
Together, these initiatives reflect Himadri’s unwavering dedication to building a supportive and empowering 
workplace. The company’s people-centric policies are not only a testament to its ethical leadership but also 
an engine for long-term success and employee satisfaction.
	
	
At Himadri, the health and well-being of our workforce remain a top priority. The Occupational Health 
Centre (OHC) plays a vital role in promoting a culture of safety, wellness, and proactive healthcare within the 
organization. It serves as a comprehensive hub for various health-related services, ensuring both employees 
and contractors receive the care and attention they need.
	
	
One of the key initiatives includes regular health checkups for contractors, ensuring that those working on-
site are medically fit and monitored periodically. In addition, periodic health checkups for employees are 
conducted systematically to track health trends and take preventive measures.
	
	
To support holistic wellness, the OHC facilitates consultations with physiotherapists for employees who 
require physical rehabilitation or recovery support. Likewise, the services of a dietitian are available for those 
seeking nutritional guidance and lifestyle management, promoting long-term health.

On-site medical attention is further strengthened by access to a plant doctor, who attends to day-to-day health 
concerns and ensures immediate consultation for any health issues arising during work hours. A dedicated 
eye checkup program for drivers ensures that vision standards are maintained, directly contributing to road 
and operational safety.
	
	
The OHC also manages the distribution of first aid medicines, providing prompt relief for minor injuries and 
ailments. Furthermore, health camps are organized periodically, encouraging wide participation and raising 
awareness about critical health issues through screenings and interactive sessions.
	
	
Together, these initiatives reflect Himadri’s commitment to not just occupational safety but overall employee 
well-being, creating a safer, healthier, and more productive work environment.

health programs along with fair working conditions reduces absenteeism and helps in employee retention. 
Programs focused on mental health support, physical well-being and stress management contribute to overall 
employee health, reducing workplace injuries and health related issues. It ensures compliance with labour laws and 
human rights standards while demonstrating a commitment to corporate social responsibility and the UN Global 
Compact as well as UN Sustainable Goals.

Himadri’s career advancement policy, nomination and remuneration policy supports professional growth equitably, 
creating long-term talent retention and satisfaction. Himadri emphasises a reward and recognition programme to 
create a positive work environment and motivate employees. We have partnered with Advantage Club to manage

resources and insights to embrace diverse perspectives. This approach leads to higher employee engagement, 
satisfaction and retention. The Company’s Nomination and Remuneration Committee supports the attraction, 
retention and motivation of high-calibre talent.
6.	
Is there a mechanism available to receive and redress grievances for the following categories of employees and 
worker? If yes, give details of the mechanism in brief.
	
Himadri has formalised and widely published its grievance mechanisms, which include a standardised hotline and 
reporting system. Relevant personnel are trained to ensure that all complaints are reviewed and escalated when 
necessary. If a complaint is justified, appropriate measures are promptly taken. Employees can report incidents 
confidentially through a toll-free number, email, or an internal portal. External stakeholders, such as contractors or 
suppliers, are also encouraged to report noncompliance. A team comprising the Chief Human Resources Officer, 
Chief Sustainability Officer and Company Secretary handles complaints with sensitivity and impartiality. Employees 
who report incidents are protected against retaliation, ensuring their safety and confidence in the system. Regular 
audits and feedback loops help identify areas for improvement and maintain a harassment-free environment. 
Whistleblowing concerns can be reported to speakup@himadri.com

Himadri’s Collective Bargaining Policy upholds the freedom of association and the effective recognition of the right 
to collective bargaining. In this context, Himadri pays importance to the rights of individual to join, form or leave a 
group voluntarily without any interference from external Parties. In Himadri we have various internal committees 
which deal with empowerment of workers, improving Working Conditions, Fair wages and benefits, Job security 
and Promotion of Social Justice results in reduction of workplace conflicts. Labor representation is mandatory in 
these committees while some of the committees are formed by management and labor representatives. However, 
joining these committees are kept voluntary for the workers and there is a pledge of no coercive actions. As a 
SA 8000:2014 certified organization, Himadri has always taken care of all who access our workplaces. Therefore, 
labour welfare committees have representation from the contractual workers as well. Our hired security forces 
are not equipped with any kind of weapon to restrict any movement of workers inside our premises. Workers are 
regularly trained on identifying workplace risks with respect to social wellbeing. These awareness sessions are 
conducted by our team with an oversight from the Board. 
	
At Himadri, the Company recognizes that open dialogue and mutual respect are foundational to creating a positive, 
fair and inclusive workplace. While no political labour unions exist within the organization, Himadri upholds the 
principles of collective bargaining through a structured and transparent approach that values the voices of all 
employees and contractors, including third-party workers. To ensure meaningful representation and engagement, 
Himadri established various employee and worker committees that serve as vital platforms for discussion, feedback 
and collaboration.

Promoting awareness of human rights and labor rights remains a key focus for Himadri. Relevant information is 
shared across the Company’s operating divisions. In addition, mandatory training is made available through the 
Learning Management System (LMS) named UTKARSH, ensuring that personnel at all locations are sensitised 
to these topics. The issue of human rights is further integrated into the Company’s existing compliance training 
programme. Himadri’s e-learning modules cover health and safety topics, allowing employees to conveniently 
complete their training. These modules ensure an alignment with the Health and Safety Policy, highlighting the 
leadership’s commitment to workplace safety. The platform offers training schedules, tracks progress and issues 
certifications to ensure that all employees. We Offer training on international safety standards, hazard identification, 
and accident prevention to ensure safer workplaces. Himadri’s engagement with British Safety Council helps 
advance workplace health and safety. The esteemed British Safety Council provides training, for employees and 
management, creating a safety-first culture.
	
Learning and development are essential success factors for promoting a strong and future-oriented company 
culture. The skills and competencies of employees are critical for profitable growth and long-term success. 
For this reason, Himadri is committed to modernising its learning culture and enhancing efforts to promote 
continuous, self-directed learning and learning from others. Employee development at Himadri is built on the 
principle that development opportunities and support are available to all employees. At Himadri, development is 
viewed as continuous learning through building individual experience and skills, further training, or job changes. 
Employees and leaders agree on these discussions during the annual employee dialogue. Employees also define 
their individual learning objectives in collaboration with their leaders as part of these ongoing conversations. 
These objectives are tailored to the specific requirements of the role and future needs. Our learning opportunities 
cater to a variety of employee development needs: starting a career, expanding knowledge, personal growth, and 
leadership development.

At Himadri, the Company believes in providing opportunities for internal talent to broaden their horizons and 
advance their careers over time. To support this, Himadri designs and offers various leadership training programmes, 
coaching and mentorship sessions and personalised career development programmes to boost employee morale. 
One such programme is PRAGATI. The objective of the PRAGATI programme is to offer identified high performers 
and high-potential individuals a platform for a fast-track learning experience, preparing them for future roles. In line 
with the Company’s current growth plans, these individuals are equipped to take on new responsibilities through 
structured learning interventions. As part of the PRAGATI initiative, participants have successfully completed the 
Executive Certification in Operations Management from IIM Vizag. The organisation has nominated participants 
for the Executive Programme in Business and Corporate Law. The General Management Course which is also a 
part of the PRAGATI initiative, is conducted monthly by industry experts, enabling participants to gain valuable 
insights into best practices within the industry. This, in turn, contributes to the organisation’s overall efficiency 
and growth. As per the latest assessment, Himadri is positioned as an ‘initiator’ on the inclusive business maturity 
curve. This milestone highlights the Company’s foundational DEI practices and establishes a strong platform for 
further advancement.
	
Bias-free hiring: Himadri employs standardised evaluations, blind resume screening and diverse interview panels 
to promote objectivity and eliminate bias in the hiring process. 
	
Talent development: Career advancement opportunities are accessible to all employees, with a focus on achieving 
equitable representation at all levels within the organisation.

a.	
Whether an occupational health and safety 
management system has been implemented by the 
entity? (Yes/ No). If yes, the coverage such system?
	
	
Yes, Himadri promotes a culture of health and 
safety while supporting labour and human 
rights. The Company prioritises the well-being 
of employees and stakeholders through the 
implementation 
of 
various 
non-negotiable 
safety standards and ethical labour practices. 
This enhances productivity and catalyses 
sustainable development. As a responsible 
chemical Company, Himadri invests in essential 
elements of health and safety practices. 
The Company has set ambitious targets and 
implemented robust measures. Key health and 
safety priorities were identified through a KPI-
driven approach. The Company emphasised the 
protection of people and property by enforcing 
health and safety protocols, measure and 
technologies designed to prevent workplace 
accidents and ill-health. This approach aligns 
with Himadri’s Zero Accident/Incident vision. 
Himadri prioritises employee well-being through 
health insurance and ESIC coverage; ESG and 
Safety Committees assess and upgrade safety 
measures. Risks are countered through controls 
that are regularly reviewed. Safety measures 
include 
advanced 
fire 
detection 
systems, 
personal protective equipment, compliance with 
regulatory standards and safe chemical handling 
procedures. The Company’s sustainability goals 
align with UNGC and UNSDGs, reflecting a 
commitment to minimise workplace injuries, 
promote well-being and develop sustainable 
practices. Himadri’s consideration of double 
materiality 
reinforces 
the 
Company’s 
commitment 
to 
understand 
and 
address 
financial and environmental/social impacts. The 
Company has mapped processes that affect 
and are influenced by  factors within its supply 
chain from upstream activities to downstream 
distribution. Double materiality comprises a 
commitment to health and safety management 
aligned 
with 
international 
and 
national 
standards, extending beyond compliance. By 
addressing challenges to business continuity, 
regulatory changes and impacts on people and 
the planet, the Company balanced profitability 
with societal and environmental responsibilities. 
This 
ensures 
proactive 
risk 
management, 
operational resilience and sustainable growth. 
	
	
OH&S Governance model -
	
	
Himadri’s OH&S matters are governed by 
ESG committee at board. The group, which 
consists 
of 
senior 
executives 
and 
board 
members, contributes a variety of knowledge 
in governance, sustainability and industry best 
practices. The Committee establishes ESG 
objectives, tracks advancement and guarantees 
compliance with international norms and laws. 
It examines and suggests methods to reduce 
the negative effects on the environment, 
encourage social responsibility and strengthen 
governance. The committee makes sure that 
the company produces sustainable growth and 
ethical business practices which increase long-
term stakeholder value by incorporating ESG 
into strategy.
	
	
At the operational level, the HSE (Health, 
Safety and Environment) and Sustainability 
Steering Committee is responsible for planning 
and executing safety-related actions across 
business units. This committee, led by unit 
heads, ensures that the corporate OH&S 
strategy is effectively implemented at plant and 
facility levels. By focusing on risk assessments, 
employee training, emergency preparedness 
and compliance with global safety standards, 
this committee acts as a bridge between 
strategic governance and on-the-ground safety 
management. The involvement of business unit 
leaders reinforces accountability and ensures 
ESG committee at Board

matters and approves the objectives.

standards and implementation.

Safety Policy promotes workplace safety with a 
zero-tolerance stance on accidents. The policy 
identifies and mitigates potential hazards. It 
emphasises physical and mental well-being. It 
promotes employee resilience and productivity. 
It makes safety a shared responsibility. 
	
	
Drug and Alcohol Policy: It prohibits the use, 
possession, or influence of drugs and alcohol 
on its premises. It enforces this policy through 
awareness programmes, confidential support 
resources and a zero-tolerance approach to 
violations. This promotes resilience among 
workers, including third-party contractors.

Risk management: Himadri’s Occupational 
Safety and Health (OSH) management is 
grounded in comprehensive risk assessment 
that 
identifies 
potential 
safety 
hazards. 
Himadri’s health and safety risk assessment and 
mitigation systematically identifies, evaluates 
and prioritises potential risks. The Company 
adheres to a risk-based approach in compliance 
with the ISO 45001:2018 and SA 8000:2014 
standards, covering all stakeholders (internal 
and external). This helps identify workplace 
risks and implement mitigation measures using 
systematic tools, reflected in lower Lost Time 
Injury Frequency Rate. The Company’s risk 
management is strategic and comprehensive, 
ensuring that all micro-level activities and 
relevant sub-activities are covered. 
	
Himadri follows five risk management steps: 
 
 
Identification of hazards;
 
 
Identification of people who might be 
harmed and how; 
 
 
Risk evaluation and precaution; 
 
 
Recording of findings;
 
 
Review and update.
	
	
These 
collaborative 
activities 
involve 
cross-functional 
departments, 
workers’ 
representatives as well as health and safety 
professionals, ensuring a holistic approach.
	
Accident and incident management
	
	
The Company’s safety performance over recent 
years illustrates sustained improvements in 
health and safety outcomes. Himadri has 
achieved measurable progress in reducing 
workplace incidents and promoting a safer 
environment. Himadri introduced a tracking 
sheet for logging injuries and incidents, with 
corrective and preventive actions shared across 
sites via a Lesson Learning Sheet (LLS). This 
helped mitigate similar risks across operations. 
The Company developed a skilled team of 80 
management employees trained in 8D Practical 
Problem Solving to investigate accidents and 
implement preventive measures.
Occupational 
health 
and 
safety 
capacity 
building
	
	
At Himadri, safety practices are marked by 
continuous 
improvement, 
periodic 
reviews 
and 
updated 
policies. 
Engaging 
workers 
(including third party) has helped percolate 
safety awareness across levels. During the 
year under review, the Company launched a 
new H&S Leadership training module, covering 
health and safety topics. During the reporting 
financial 
year, 
the 
Company 
covered 
all 
management category employees. Himadri 
prioritised a new Permit to- Work standard, 
training relevant employees and deploying it 
across divisions, integrating risk management 
into the system. The Company adopted the 8D 
(Eight Disciplines) Practical Problem Solving 
(PPS) method, a structured tool in accident and 
incident investigations. This method identifies 
root causes and implements corrective actions. 
Management 
employees 
received 
8D-PPS 
training to investigate incidents and implement 
solutions. 
	
	
During the last financial year, Himadri conducted 
approximately 25,018 man hours of safety 
training (classroom sessions, online courses, 
hands-on drills, interactive workshops and 
modules on its Utkarsh Learning Management 
System). This covered employees, workers 
and third-party contractors, and consumed an 
average 12 hours per person per year.

Monitoring and auditing for continual improvement:
	
	
Himadri’s rigorous approach to health and safety is marked by quarterly audits that cover key ESG areas. 
These audits are led by qualified internal auditors and members of the Health, Safety and Environment team. 
Regular evaluations are conducted across the Company’s manufacturing sites, with a focus on Safety Audits, 
Risk Assessment, Health and Safety Training and KPI-related action plans. In addition to quarterly internal 
audits, Himadri conducts annual external audits and third-party assessments on key statutory provisions, 
including IS 14489, which addresses Occupational Health and Safety management system. Moreover we 
periodically conducts Electrical Safety and Fire Safety Audits (third party) following national and international 
regulations. This layered audit structure helps the Company adhere to high Health and Safety management 
standards. By integrating internal audits, external reviews and third-party assurance, Himadri has established 
a comprehensive framework that promotes transparency, accountability and improvement. This approach 
empowers the Company to communicate advancements towards health and safety Management.
	
	
Himadri offers a number of procedures and 
platforms for employees to formally report 
work-related risks. The Safety Audit Tool is 
one such tool that our employees use on the 
job. Every week, all Himadri employees take 
part in the workplace audit and report issues 
to the relevant department for resolution. We 
have introduced a QR Code-based reporting 
system to make it easier for employees to 
report work-related hazards. Over 32 percent 
of our employees’ participation increased in FY 
24-25 who conducts regular safety audits on a 
monthly basis. In FY 24-25 we have captured 
over 9,638 number of safety audit points which 
has increased from 4,117 Safety Audit Points 
from the last FY 23-24. Moreover, the closure rate 
also increased to 86.5% overall which includes 
various Safety Improvement Opportunities 
(SIO) to upgrade the Safety Standard.
	
	
This led to an overall improvement in worker 
safety. Employees are involved in this audit 
program, including line managers, employees, 
top management and HSE staff. We will be 
applying the same rule to temporary and 
contract workers in the future.

b.	
What are the processes used to identify work-related hazards and assess risks on a routine and non-routine 
basis by the entity?
	
	
Himadri’s occupational health strategy is structured around comprehensive safety initiatives. This encompasses 
risk assessment, standardisation of procedures, workplace health promotion, occupational health training, 
occupational hygiene management, occupational health services, rehabilitation and institutional support 
for work-related injuries / illnesses and audits (internal and external). The focus is on identifying potential 
hazards, assessing risks, establishing safety protocols and supporting wellbeing (physical and mental). Himadri 
emphasises hygiene standards, offers medical support and provides support (rehabilitation and institutional). 
This holistic approach underlines Himadri’s dedication to sustain a safe and healthy work environment. Risk 
assessment is key to occupational health at Himadri, ensuring the identification, evaluation and mitigation of 
workplace health hazards to protect employee safety and well-being. This process begins with identifying 
potential hazards, assessing their likelihood and severity and implementing control measures to reduce risks. 
Himadri’s general risk assessment comprises identifying, capturing and recording occupational health risks.
	
	
Himadri has implemented a comprehensive standard operating procedure (Framework) to manage industrial 
noise effectively, ensuring a safe, compliant and comfortable work environment for all employees. Several 
impactful noise reduction measures have already been implemented. For instance, acoustic hoods have been 
installed in high-noise areas such as the CETP and RC zones. Through continuous noise monitoring and the 
adoption of advanced noise mitigation technologies, the Company strives to reduce its environmental impact 
while supporting a quieter, safer workspace.
	
	
Risk assessment is key to occupational health at Himadri, ensuring the identification, evaluation and mitigation 
of workplace health hazards to protect employee safety and well-being. This process begins with identifying 
potential hazards, assessing their likelihood and severity and implementing control measures to reduce 
risks. Himadri’s general risk assessment comprises identifying, capturing and recording occupational health 
risks. Risks are categorised into high, medium and low levels based on the likelihood of prolonged exposure. 
High and medium risks are reviewed monthly by the senior management in the ESG Council level to ensure 
proactive oversight. Himadri prioritises controls, including elimination, reduction, isolation and exposure 
control. Personal protective equipment is provided at no cost to all employees and contractors, reinforcing 
the Company’s health-conscious environment.

Standard Activities-These are divided into 
repetitive 
and 
periodic 
categories. 
The 
process for managing standard and non-
standard activities enhances the safety focus. 
For standard activities, which occur either 
repetitively or periodically, the process begins 
with risk assessment to identify and mitigate 
potential hazards. Detailed instructions are 
developed to ensure safe operations and that 
employees undergo training and validation to 
confirm their related competence. The process is 
reviewed annually. Himadri’s Standardised Work 
Instructions (SWIs) provide a comprehensive 
framework that ensures consistency across 
operations. These SWIs are based on internal 
standards that are aligned with EN and ISO 
standards. The key elements of the SWIs 
include:

to

to

environmental impact through sustainable 
approaches.	
	
	
	
Non-standard (non-routine) activities-Himadri 
addresses non-routine work through its Permit 
to Work (PTW) system. This structured process 
identifies, 
communicates, 
mitigates 
and 
controls risks in hazardous areas, non-standard 
situations and potentially dangerous conditions 
(shutdowns), enhancing frontline worker safety. 
In the Company’s 24x7 operations, PTW system 
is mandatory, typically used in maintenance. Non-
standard activities, while frequent, are exceptional 
and require a customised approach. These activities 
commence with risk assessment to address 
specific and unique risks. Before proceeding, PTW 
ensures safety. Workers are trained and participate 
in toolbox talks (TBT) to manage associated risks. 
There are seven main types of work permits: Hot 
work permits, General work permits, Confined 
spaces work permits, Electrical work permits, 
Height work permits, Excavation permits and 
Radiography work permits. Each work permit is 
categorised based on the nature of the job and 
associated hazards, ensuring appropriate safety 
measures are implemented.

c. 	
Whether you have processes for workers to 
report the work related hazards and to remove 
themselves from such risks. (Y/N)
	
	
Yes, Himadri established multiple channels for 
workers to report work-related hazards. A key 
tool for this purpose is the Safety Audit Tool, 
used by employees to enhance workplace 
safety. Each week, all employees participate in 
workplace audits and promptly escalate any 
identified issues to the relevant department 
for correction. To simplify reporting, Himadri 
introduced a QR code-based reporting system, 
enabling employees to easily raise work-related 
hazard reports. Employees can access digital 
safety checklists and receive real-time updates 
on safety protocols and corrective status.
	
	
Himadri addresses the timely reporting of 
incidents (fires, explosions, material spills and 
other chemical releases). Himadri’s internal 
accident and incident reporting standards 
adopt stringent definitions for Lost Time 
Injuries (LTIs) and severe accidents compared 
to regulatory bodies. All manufacturing plants 
are required to report medically treated Injuries 
(MTIs), extending investigations to include all 
Dangerous Occurrences (DOs) and MTIs. Himadri 
investigates every accident and incident in its 
manufacturing plants and offices. First-aid cases 
and low severity DOs are addressed through 
the Line Practical Problem Solving tool, while 
MTIs, RSIs, LTIs and high severity DOs involving 
process-related incidents are managed using 
the 8D Practical Problem Solving (PPS) tool. 
The Company employs an internally developed 
incident reporting tool to communicate incidents 
to stakeholders across its manufacturing sites. 
Himadri targeted to reach a Lost Time Injury 
Frequency Rate (LTIFR) of below 1.0.
	
	
Comprehensive approach in Safety Audit and 
Risk Assessment - Himadri adopts a proactive 
approach to safety audits to find out the safety 
improvement opportunities (SIOs) and conclude 
with their preventive actions. In addition to 
it, workplace risk assessments particularly 
emphasizing risks with a Risk Priority Number 
(RPN) above 32 were conducted on regular 
basis to initiate actions and their closure for all 
the work related high risk areas. Such high-RPN 
scenarios indicate substantial risk and Himadri’s 
policies prioritize these areas to ensure effective 
control measures and mitigation strategies. 
Regular safety audits, in alignment with internal 
standards evaluate these risk zones to identify 
potential threats and enhance safety measures. 
This approach integrates continuous monitoring, 
assessment and improvement protocols aiming 
to safeguard both employee and non-employee 
workers through detailed action plans, training 
and regular follow-ups of audit points and 
their closure which is termed as SIOPA (Safety 
Improvement Opportunities with permanent 
Actions) in Himadri to manage risks effectively 
and uphold a secure work environment. 841 
nos. of total risk were identified for FY 24-25 in 
comparison to 471 nos. of total risks which were 
identified during FY 23-24 with high risk being 
440 in numbers. Closure percentage of all the 
risk captured from Risk Assessment is lying at 
83.82% and in FY 24-25 we have captured over 
9,638 number of safety audit points which has 
increased from 4,117 Safety Audit Points from 
the last FY 23-24. Moreover, the closure rate 
also increased to 86.5% overall which includes 
various Safety Improvement Opportunities 
(SIO) to upgrade the Safety Standard.

d. 	 Do the employees/ worker of the entity have access to non-occupational medical and health care services? 
(Yes/ No)
	
	
Yes, Himadri, as a responsible employer, recognizes the importance of supporting the overall health and well-
being of  its employees, extending beyond work-related injuries or illnesses. The company offers comprehensive 
health insurance plans, which cover a variety of healthcare services, including routine doctor visits, specialist 
consultations, prescription medications and preventive care services such as vaccinations and health screenings. 
Additionally, Himadri organizes regular health check-up camps and wellness programs, allowing employees to 
proactively monitor their health and address any concerns early. For mental health support, the company offers 
Employee Assistance Programs that provides confidential counselling services to help employees manage 
personal or work related stress, anxiety and other mental health challenges. The approach to address the same 
is multi stepped, which imply Identification of work related stresses, Assessment of impact, Categorization 
of impact, Measurement, Monitoring and improvement. Mindfulness and stress reduction activities (yoga, 
meditation, or breathing exercises) are promoted. Workshops on time management, stress-reduction techniques 
and resilience equip employees with strategies for handling pressure.

Employees feel more valued and cared for by the organization when it is transparent about any safety concerns or 
accidents. It signals to all stakeholders that safety is a priority and that they organization is dedicated to addressing 
and preventing risks. This promotes safety culture where employees feel empowered to report potential hazards 
and are actively involved in maintaining a safe work environment.
	
Himadri’s e-learning modules cover health and safety topics, allowing employees to conveniently complete their 
training. These modules ensure an alignment with the Health and Safety Policy, highlighting the leadership’s 
commitment to workplace safety Himadri’s QR code-enabled mobile application empowers employees to conduct 
safety audits, report hazards and submit safety concerns from smartphones. This application supports daily 
compliance with Tool Box Talk protocols and facilitates root cause analysis for accidents, engaging all relevant 
departments and individuals. Employees can access digital safety checklists and receive real-time updates on 
safety protocols and corrective status. Through these digital tools, Himadri promotes a technology-driven safety 
culture which has helped to reduce safety related incidents.
	
The continue decline in the numbers of safety incidents over years, signifies our diligent efforts at imparting non-
negotiable safety norms at workplace, further emphasizing our Sustainability objective of ‘zero accident’ vision. 
Strong health and safety policy has minimized the risk of accidents, injuries and occupational diseases.
	
As per Himadri’s Accident and Incident reporting standard we report LTIs Work-related fatality, injury or 
occupational illness/disease resulting in the loss of 1 full day or more, not including the day or shift on which the 
accident occurred. If the day following the incident is a non-working day, the incident is still an LTI if the person is 
not fit for work.
12.	 Describe the measures taken by the entity to ensure a safe and healthy work place
	
	
Himadri 
takes 
a 
robust 
and 
systematic 
approach to occupational safety, prioritizing 
the well-being and security of its employees, 
contractors, and all stakeholders involved in its 
operations. The company follows a structured 
safety 
framework 
encompassing 
multiple 
interconnected components that ensure a safe, 
healthy, and resilient workplace.
	
1. 	
Risk Assessment
	
	
The foundation of Himadri’s safety culture 
begins 
with 
proactive 
risk 
assessment. 
Potential hazards are systematically identified 
and evaluated to implement effective control 
measures that prevent workplace incidents.

2. 	 Management Standards and Non-Standard 
Works
	
	
The company sets stringent management 
standards and pays special attention to non-
standard or high-risk tasks. This ensures 
that every work activity, especially those 
outside routine operations, is carried out with 
appropriate safety protocols.
	
3. 	 Workplace Safety
	
	
Physical workplace conditions are continuously 
monitored and improved to eliminate unsafe 
conditions. Himadri ensures safe infrastructure, 
proper ergonomics, and adherence to safety 
guidelines to reduce injury risks.
	
4. 	 Contractor Safety Management
	
	
Safety is extended beyond employees to 
include all third-party contractors. Himadri 
ensures contractors comply with internal safety 
requirements 
through 
induction 
programs, 
monitoring, and audits.
	
5. 	 Accident and Incident Management
	
	
Any 
incident, 
no 
matter 
how 
minor, 
is 
thoroughly investigated. Root cause analyses 
are conducted, and corrective actions are 
implemented 
to 
prevent 
recurrence 
and 
promote a culture of continuous improvement.
	
6. 	 Emergency Management
	
	
Preparedness is key. Himadri conducts regular 
emergency drills and has response systems in 
place to manage fires, chemical leaks, and other 
emergencies, 
thereby 
minimizing 
potential 
harm to people and property.
	
7. 	
Engagement of Workforce
	
	
A strong safety culture is built on employee 
involvement. 
Workers 
are 
encouraged 
to 
participate in safety committees, report hazards, 
and contribute suggestions for improving 
workplace safety.
	
8. 	 Occupational Safety Capacity Building
	
	
Continuous 
training 
and 
capacity-building 
programs 
are 
implemented 
to 
enhance 
employees’ knowledge and competence in 
safety practices. This includes technical training, 
behavioral safety programs, and leadership 
engagement.
	
9. 	 External/Internal Auditing, Procedure and 
Review
	
	
Regular audits, both internal and external, are 
conducted to assess compliance with safety 
standards. These audits help identify gaps and 
guide the necessary procedural improvements. 
Himadri implemented internal safety audit 
standard where the participation percentage 
increased by 33% than the last financial year.
	
10. 	 Rewards and Recognition
	
	
Himadri recognizes and rewards individuals 
and teams who contribute significantly to 
safety improvements. This not only motivates 
employees but reinforces the value of safe 
behavior in the organization.

12. 	 Act on Opportunities for Continual Improvement
	
Safety is not static; Himadri continually seeks opportunities for enhancement. Through lessons learned, 
benchmarking, and technological innovations, the company strives to elevate its safety performance.
	
Himadri is committed to complying with all local, national and international health and safety regulations. Regular 
updates on changes to safety laws are communicated to employees and integrated into the company’s safety 
practices. The company ensures that all safety protocols and practices align with the legal requirements.
	
Himadri’s occupational health strategy is structured 
around 
comprehensive 
safety 
initiatives. 
This 
encompasses 
risk 
assessment, 
standardization 
of 
procedures, 
workplace 
health 
promotion, 
occupational health training, occupational hygiene 
management, 
occupational 
health 
services, 
rehabilitation and institutional support for work-
related injuries / illnesses and audits (internal and 
external). The focus is on identifying potential 
hazards, assessing risks, establishing safety protocols 
and supporting wellbeing (physical and mental). 
Himadri emphasizes hygiene standards, offers 
medical support and provides support (rehabilitation 
and institutional). This holistic approach underlines 
Himadri’s dedication to sustain a safe and healthy 
work environment. Himadri’s Anti-Discrimination 
and Harassment Policy, outlines our stance against 
discrimination and harassment prohibiting any 
behavior such as verbal abuse, inappropriate jokes, 
unwelcome advances and defines measures for 
ensuring compliance, addressing violations, and 
fostering a safe work environment for all employees. 
	
Himadri 
prioritizes 
occupational 
health 
by 
identifying, evaluating, and mitigating workplace 
health hazards to protect employee safety and well-
being. The process involves identifying potential 
hazards, assessing their likelihood and severity, and 
implementing control measures to reduce risks. 
Himadri categorizes risks into high, medium, and 
low levels based on prolonged exposure likelihood. 
High and medium risks are reviewed monthly by 
senior management, while controls like elimination, 
reduction, isolation, and exposure control are 
prioritized. 
Personal 
protective 
equipment 
is 
provided free of charge to all employees and 
contractors.
	
Himadri is committed to implementing occupational 
health standards to ensure workplace safety and 
employee well-being. These standards align with 
national and international regulations, and Himadri 
conducts regular risk assessments to identify 
potential workplace health hazards. The company 
prioritizes improvements in areas with the highest 
potential risks. Workplace health programs focus on 
stress management, noise control, and ergonomics, 
enhancing employees' physical and mental health, 
increasing 
morale, 
and 
reducing 
absenteeism. 
Occupational health services are central to Himadri, 
providing medical support, routine health checks, 
and wellness programs. Regular training and 
education on occupational health ensures staff are 
informed about health and safety standards and 
equipped to handle workplace risks. By implementing 
occupational health standards, Himadri promotes 
a safe, healthy, and supportive workplace, ensuring 
long-term wellbeing and protection from potential 
hazards.
